Ingi gwa u Yesu akapiluka akamuila Petro, “Suka kitalane mulugu uewe weenda ngilya kitalane, kunsoko shangaukee ulukani lang'wi Tunda, endu kee zizi niantu du.”
Sunga u Yesu akaila iamanyisigwa akwe ang'wi muntu wihi nuloilwe kuntyata iime ihi namunkumbigulu, ahole uhuili wakwe, sunga antyate.
Uyu nuloilwe kuuguna upanga wa mihi ukulimilya, nuyu wihi kumalimilya kunsoko ane ukamaguna.
Ukupata nsao ki umuntu aga amipate ihi hi kunu alimilye upanga wake? Kintu kii nukuila nuupanga wakwe?
Kululo ung'wana wang'wa Adamu uzile nuukulu wang'wa Tata akwe nia malaika akwe, ng'wenso uze apa ikinyamulimo iantu kukiila witumi wao.
Tai kumuila akoli apa ianyu niimikile singaaziza mionza insha sunga azizamuona ung'wa wang'wa Adamu nuzile muutemi wakwe.
Mahiku mutandatu u Yesu akahola palung'wi nung'wenso Prtro nu Yakobo, nu Yohana muluna wakwe, hangi akahola akaatwala migulya mlugulu nululepu.
Au kaiwe pa ntongeela ao, uso wakwe ukamiliginta anga ilyoa, nu nguo yakwe ikigela ikazemiliginta anga uwelu.
Pang'wanso ikapumila Musa nu Eliya akazeligitya nung'wenso.
U Petro akasusha akamuila u Yesu, Mukulu, ukutula iza ne usese kutula ang'we uloilwe kuizenga itali itatumking'wi kang'wa kako, king'wi kunsoko ang'wa Musa ni king'wi kunsoko ang'wa Eliya.”
Itungo naakuligitya ilunde lyelu likaguma mululi, likapumula luli milunde lukazelunga, “Uyu ingi ng'wana mulowa nindoigwe, mtegeeli.”
Iamanyisigwa akwe naiija nanso, akagwa undala pihi akogopa.
Sunga u Yesu akaza akaamba, akalunga, uki hangi leki kogopi.
Nienso ikahumbula imiho ao migulya singa ikamuona anga muntu, ikamuona u Yesu du.
Naikusima mulugulu u Yesu akaapa ilagilo, akalunga, “Muleki kupumya ukunukuilwa sunga nu ng'wana wang'wa Adamu nuzeuka kupuma kuashi.”
Iamanyisigwa akwe akamukolya kuniki iakilisi akulunga u Eliya akutongela kiza atule wang'wandyo?
U Yesu akasusha akalunga, u Eliya uzile itai hangi ukususha inkani yihi.
Kululo numuie unye, u Eliya wahumile kiza, shaikamumanya, ikamulendeela inkani nialoilwe enso. Ni ite ung'wana wang'wa Adamu uzizagigwa mumikono ao.
Sunga iamanyisigwa akwe ikalinga kina aukuligitya nkani ya Yohana Mbatizaji.
Naapika mumilundo wa antu, muntu ung'wi akamuhanga, akatugama pantongeela akwe akamuila,
“Mukulu muhumile kinyauwai ung'waane, kunsoko izutite lyagu la kugwa nkolo, wiza aze gwa mumyongo nu mumazi.
Ai numuletile kuamanyisigwa ako singa ikamuguna.
U Yesu akasukiilya, akalunga, “Unye wileli nishauhuie hangi nikigazikile kikie nunye sunga nali?” Muleti apa ninkoli.
U Yesu akamupatya, nu mintunga akahega. Umuhumba akagunika imatungo yao.
Sunga iamanyisigwa ikamuhanga u Yesu kinkunku ikamukolya, kuniki kahita kuhuma kumuzunsa umintunga?
Yesu akaaila kunsoko auhuili wanyu unino, tai numuie ang'wi mukutula nuhuili unino anga uluseke nula mbeu a haraali, muhumile kuila ulugulu hega apa ulongole uko, nuenso ukuhama kutili kintu kihi nikikulemeka kung'wanyu.
Ingi gwa impyani iyi naa mintunga shehuma kuhega, ihega kukiila malompi nukiima. (shayigee muilingasilyo ninza nia kali).
Matungo naiakili akoli ku Galilaya u Yesu akaaila iamanyisigwa akwe, ung'wana wang'wa Adamu ukutula mumikono aantu.
Hangi akumubulaga nu luhiku lakatatu ukuuka, iamanyisigwa ikahungwa kinyauwai.
Naiapika ku Kapernaumu antu ahoela mpia nusu shekeli akamuhanga u Petro nukulunga, umumanyisi anyu wilipa ne inusu shekeli?
Akalunga ee, u Petro nai wingila munyumba akwe, u Yesu akaligitya nu Petro akalunga, ukusiga ntuni Simoni? Iatemi amihi ihoela impia, angwi kung'wa nyeni? Ang'wi kuantu nizaa temile kupuma kuageni?
Nu Petro nauliye, kupuma kuageni u Yesu akamuila kululo awa niakoli muutemi ahegigwe mulipi.
Kululo kuleke kuitumya iahoela mpia, itume milandu, longola muluzi goma indoano, na umihole insamaki iyo na ng'wandyo, naiwalugula umulomo wakwe, ukuhanga mumo impia ing'wi. Imihole uape iahoela mpia kunsoko ane nuewe.
Matungo yayoyayo iamanyisigwa akaza kung'wa Yesu akamuila, Nyenyu numukulu muutemi akigulu?
Yesu akamitanga umung'enya numunino, akamuika pakati ao.
Akahinga, tai numuie, iga muhite kila itunu nukutula anga ang'enya nianino singamuzizahuma kingila ku utemi wa kigulu.
Kululo uyu nuituna anga ng'wana numunino, Umuntu nuanso mukulu kutemi nuakigulu.
Nuyu wihi nuimu singiilya unge'wana numunino unsingiilyenene.
Kululo wihi nukuhuma kukinyila kuantuawa nianino nizaahui kumuleka Itunda. Ikutula iza umuntu nuanso atungiligwe igwe la kusela munkingo agumilwe mulunzi nululundu.
Isatiko lanyu anyaunkumbingula kunsoko a nkani ya unkunyili, kunsoko aya aiwi azizaimatungo. Ingi gwa isaliko lakwe umuntu uyu nuziziza kumatungo ayo, naziziza kunsoko ane.
Ang'wi umukono wako numugulu weenda kukinyila, Uteme uugume kuli nu ewe, hangi ikutula iza kitalako kingila kuupanga uzewimugila umukono ang'wi wimlema, kukila kungungwa kumoto uzazitite umikono nimigulu ihi.
Ang'wi iliho liko likutosha lipe uligume kuli nuewewe, ukutula iza uewe kingila ni liho lingwi kukola kwingila ni miho abiilikunu endu soswe moto.
Gozi mleke kumudalaha ung'wi wa anino awa. kunsoko kumuila kina kilunde akale amalaika ao mahiku ihi azeaulindie uunso wang'wa Tata ane nua kigulu.

Mukusiga ntuni? iga itule umuntu utite nkolo igana ling'wi ilimile ing'wi singi ukualeka ne ao ni makumi kenda mulugulu nukulongola kumupenza uyo nung'wi?
Anga amuhole, tai kumuila, ukulumbilya kukila ao ni makumi kenda na kenda ni singa aialimie.
Ingi iti singa ulowa wang'wa Tata anyu nuakigulu kina ung'wi waanino awa kulimansila.
Ang'wi ng'waanyu wakulea, longola ende umuhugulye uewe nu ng'wenso anga akije waina munyandugu ako.
Anga wahita kuulegeelya, muhole muntu ng'wi ang'wi abiili palung'wi nue, kunsoko imilomo naantu abiili ang'wi atatu ihumile kukondanilya ulukani luzipe.
Anga wihita kumutegeelya liile itekeelo ulukani ulu, angawahila hangi kulilegeelya itekeelo, nuanso waina munya kilungu rumuhoela mpia.
Tai numuile kilu nimukukilungaila mihi nu kilunde kikulugailwa hangi kilu nimukukilugula mihi nukigulu kikuhugulwa.
Hangi numuie kina antu abiili miumbi lanyu anga igombye lukani lihi mihi nialulompila nulanso utata ane nuakigulu ukituma.
Kunsoko abiili ang'wi atatu nikie palung'wi kukiila lina lane, nunene nkoli palung'wi nienso.
Hangi u Petro akaza akamuila u Yesu, ''mukulu, umunyanduguani antashe kanga nune numulekee, ata mupangati?
U Yesu akamuila, singakuila ang'wi mupugati, Ingi ata iti imakumi mupungati na mupungati.
Kunsoko nanso utemi wa kigulu wilika nuulemi uo nautakile kunonelya ialo la mutugwa wakwe.
Naiwandya kunonelya ialo, umutugwe akwe ung'wi anudaiye makumi anzagu ikumi.
Kunsoko aimugila anga nzila akulipa, unugole akwe akalagiilya aguligwe umusungu akwe, palung'wi niana akwe ni kintu kihi nautile uulipe wifung'we.
Umutugwa akagwa, akatugama pa ntongeela akwe, akalunga mukulu utule nuugimya palung'wi nune hangi kuulipa kila ikintu.
Umugole wang'wa mutugwa nuanso akahungwa kinyauwai akalekanuka nayo ihi naumudaiye.
Ingigwa umutugwa naiwalekelwa numugole, akalongola akamuamba muntungwi akamgoga kunsoka amudailye dinari igana ling'wi, akamuila ndipe iko ninukudaiye.
Umutugwa uyu naudaigwe akamuila nindiile kuupa udu aya nundailye.
Umuntu gwa uyu nuang'wandyo akahita, sunga akalongola akamutunga kukitungo, anga wazawamailya iko numudaiye amutunguile.
Latugwa niangiza naiaona nikanso makipumie, Ikahung'wa kinyauwai kikulu, akaza ikamuila umugole ao kihi iko naikine kung'wanso.
Ingi gwa umgole uyo nua mutugwa akamitango akamuila ue mutugwa numbi, nakalekela uewe ideni lake lili kunsoko aumpepeye.
Uewe gwa? singa au humile na kutula ni kinyauwai kumutugwa miako? Anga une nainukumie ikinyauwai.
Umugole akwe ataka akamutwala kuantu niaja iantu, akatula gigwa sunga ruzemaila ilipo naudaigwe.
Iti ingi uu uTata ane nuakigulu uzimu tendeela, ang'wi ung'wianyu shuzemulekela imilandu umulana akwe kupuma munkolo yanyu.
U Yesu naiwakondya kuligitya inkani izi, akahega ku Galilaya, hangi akalongola mumpolempole a Yudea kuntongeela amongo wa Jordani.
Mihundo ukulu wa antu ukamutyata, ukapantika uguniki kuko.
Mafarisayo akamuhanga u Yesu, akamugema, akamuila, Ikutula taine umuntu kumuleka umusungu akwe kunsoko ihi?
U Yesu asusha akalunga, ''shamusomile ne kina uyu nauauimbile ung'wandyo, auaumbile mitinja nu musungu?
Hangi akalunga, kunsoko iye umitunja ukumuleka utata akwe nu iakwe nukutula palung'wi numusungu akwe nianso abiili akatula muili ung'wi.
Kuluko singa abiili hangi, aina muili ung'wi ingi gwa iko naukikamantilye Itunda, kutile muntu wihi nukukikamantula.
Ikamuiila niki gwa umusa aupamilye ilago li tutu nulakumuleka?
Akaaila kunsoko aukaku wa nkolo yanyu, umusa akaagombya kualike iasungu ao ingigwa kupuma ng'wandyo singa aiza uu.
Numuie kina wihi nukumuleka umusungu akwe angwe singa nsoko augoolya nukutina musungu mungiza, ukutula wagoolya, numitunja nukumutina umu sungu naulekilwe la ukutula wagoolya.
Amwanyisigwa akamuila u Yesu ang'wi uu yili umugoha nu musungu singa iziza kutina.
U Yesu akaila ingi singa kila munti uhumile kusingiilya umanyisi uwu ingi aoiti dunia gombigwe kusingiilya.
Kululo gwa akoli iantu naiaimilwe uhumi wa kituma ikimuili, kupuma niang'wi aiaimilwe uhumi nuanso niantu, niang'wi aimpya nilye age kunsoko itume lukani la kigulu, nuhumile kusingiilya umanyisigwa ausingiilye.
Sunga akatwaila ang'enya anino alume kuaikilya imikono ao nu kulompa iamanyisigwa akwe ikamupatya.
U Yesu akaila, ''agombi'' iangenya nianino, laki kuagili kuza kitalame, kunsoko uetemi wa kigulu ingi wa antu anga wawa.
Nung'wenso akaika imikono akwe migulya ao, sunga akahega pang'wanso.
Muntu ung'wi akaza kung'wa Yesu akalunga, ''mumanyisi, kintuni nikiza nini humile kituma sunga mpanlike utemi nuakali nakali.
U Yesu akamuila, kuniki nukunkolya ikintu kinikiza? Ukoli ung'wi du numuza, ang'wi uloilwe kupantika uupanga ambiila uunonelya wa ng'wi Tunda.
Umuntu nuanso akamukolya, unonelya kii? u Yesu akalunga, leka kubalaga, leka kugoolya, leka kia, leka kuligitya uleele.
Akulye utata ako nuiako, hangi mulowe umanyakisali anga uewe nizawiloilwe.
Umuntu nuanso akamuila, aya ihi nimakondaniye. Nikiule ni mpee.
U Yesu akamuila ang'wi uloilwe kukondanila, longola ende ugulye ihi uape iahimbe ukutula ni kiuto kihunde, sunga nzuu untyate.
Umuhumba yu naiwija ayo nu Yesu naukumuila akahenga akazesiga masigo idu, kunsoko aiwilingie nsao yidu.
U Yesu akaila iamanyisigwa akwe; '' Tai numuiie ikaku umugole kingila muutemi wa kigulu.
Hangi numuie ingi ipepeele ingami kukiila mibolomyo la sindano, kukila umugole kingila mutemi wa kigulu.
Iamanyisigwa naiija nanso, ikakuilwa nangulu nukulunga, ''Nyenyu gwa nuzegunika?
U Yesu akaagoza akalunga, kuantu shalihumikile, kung'wi Tunda ihi nanso ahumile.
Sunga u Petro akamusukiilya akamuila, Goza, kaleka ihi kakatyata uewe, kintu ki nikupantika kitalako?
Yesu akaila, ''Tai numuie, uyu nuantyatile unene muileli nupya mumatungo na ng'wana wang'wa Adamu, nuzizikie pakatikati pi tundu la ukulu wa mukola, nunye muzizikie migulya amatundu ikumi na abiili na ukulu kumapa ulamulwa makabila ikumi na abiili na Israel.
Sunga ung'wi anyu naulekile ito lakwe, aluna niagoha, nawa niasungu, Tata, ia, ana ang'wi mugunda kunsoko a lina lane, ukusingiilya kukila igana, nu kusala uutemi nuakali nakali.
Idu awa niang'wandyo itungili, azetula anyuma, nawa nianyuma azizatula angwandyo.
Kumdogoilyo utemi nuakilunde ukimpyananu muntu nukete umugunda, nai wiandiie ukedaudau nsoko akuaika anyamilimo mumugunda wakwe nuamizabibu.
Nae igombya neanyamilemo dinalu ing'wi kumung'wi, wikaayuma ende kumugunda nua mezabibu.
Nai akeile masaa ataatu wikenda hange uu wikaaona itumi angiza aeimekule akeeze agila anga mulemo pake awiza kisoko.
Wikaaila, ''Nunyenye gwa, longoli mumugunda nuamuzabibu, hange kehi nemutakile kumupa Uuu ekalongola kitumia umulemo.
Wikalongola hange naakela masaa mutandatu muma saa nemutandatu, wikituma uulukulu.
Nkua yedu hange naepikile saa ikumi neleng'wi akenda nukuahanga eantu neangiza imekile akeze angila anga mulemo. Wikaaila, ''kuneke mumehile apa nuagile anga mulemo wehi kuluhiku lehi?
Ika muila kunsoko kutile umuntu wehi nukupee umulemo. Wika aila nunyenye gaa lungoli mumugunda nua mezabibu.
Imatungo ampinde napikile, umuhola mugunda nua mezabibu wikamuila umemeeli wakwe, ''Itange eitumi wape ekinyamulimo, kandiilya nua musho sunga nua nguandyo.
Nae ekiza awa nae aikilwe saa kumi ne ng'wi, kelaung'wi ausengiiye dinali.
Nae ekiza eitumi ang'wandyo, aeasigike kena akupegwa kukele, kuite ekasingiilyegua kela ung'wi dinali ing'wi kela umuntu.
Nae ikasingiilya dunyamulimo kao, ikamisusumelya umukola mugunda.
Ikalunga, ''Ee eitumi neampelo aeitumiile isaa Ing'wi udu muitumi mulemo kuite waempyania nusese use kukenkile imeligo kuluhuku lelinukupya mpasui.
Kuite umuhola nuugunda wihesusha nukulunga kung'wi wao, muhumbe miane, singa nutumile anga ubii.
Itee? singa aelugombilyene nunene kudinali eng'wi?
Itee singa taine leung'wane kutuma anga nendilwe ninsao yane? Ang'wi iliho lako ibe nsoho une nemuza?
Unu nua mwisho ukutula wang'wendyo nuyu nua ng'wandyo ukutula wa mwisho.
U Yesu nauhunankila kena kuyelusalemu awahoile iamanyisigwa akwe ikumi nuubiili kumpelo, numunzila wikaaila.
Gozi kuunaikela kuyelusalemu, nu Ng'wana wang'wa Adamu uhukwa mumikono aakulu aakuhani neaandeki. Akumulamuila ensha.
Hange akamupunya kuantu ne amahi nsoko kumumela, kumukua nukumutumbeka. Kuite uluhiku laka taatu ukuiuka.
Hange uia nua ng'wana wang'wa Zebedayo ae uzile kung'wa Yesu niana akwe. Wikatungama ntongeela akwe nukulompa kentu kupuma kung'waakwe.
U Yesu wika nuila, ''utakile ntuni? Wikamuiila, ''Lunga kena iana ane neabiiliikie, ung'wi kumohono wako nua hegoha hange ung'wi kumokono wako nua kekema nuuitemi wako''
Kuite u Yesu wihasusha nululunga, ''singauine eke nukulompa. Itee? Uhumilene kung'wela ekekole nekung'wela? ekamuila''Kuuhuma''
Aaaila, ekehole kane mukuhingwela. Kuite kikie umukono wane nua kulela numokono wane nuakekema singa anga nene kumupa, kuite kuawa neanoneeigwe nutata wane''.
Eamanyisigwa neangeza ikuminaeigule uu, iha ambwa ukea nea luna ao neabiili.
Kuite u Yesu wikaitanga ung'wenso nukuaile, ''Muleugile kena eahumu nea mihe amuduile, nea hulu ao ituma uuhumi kitalao.
Kuite ileke kutula uu kitulanyu kuleka ite, wehi nakulowa kutula mukulu nulalanyu kusinjawatule mutumi wanyu.
Nunyu nukulula wang'wendyo kusinja watu mitumi wanyu.
Anga uu ung'wana nuang'wa Adamu singa ae uzitumilwa inge kituma, nukupunya uupanga wakwe kutule ukomoli waantu duu.''
Imatungo naeapumile kuyeliko, iimbe ikulu lekamityata.
Hange ika aona apoku abiili ikie mumpelompelo anzila. Naeigule kena Uyesu ukukela, ekitanta mduli ekalunga, ''Mukulu, Ng'wana wang'wa Daudi ukugeze.''
Kuite iumbe likaakenda nukuaila kulagi. Ata uu, neanso ekahulya unduli kukile nukulunga '' Mukulu Ng'wana wang'wa Daudi kugoze.''
Hange u Yesu wikenuka wikailanga nukuaholya mutakile numulendele ulee?
Ikamuila, ''Mukulku kena emiho itu apelye.
Inge u Yesu wikalutwe nuukea, wika maambaemiho ao, inge uu ekasingiilya uhumi wakuona hange ikanityata.
U Yesu neamanyisigwa akwa ekapika pakupi ne Yelusalemu hange ekalongola sunga kuBethfage, kulugulu nuka mezeituni, hange u Yesu wihaatuma iamanyisigwa abiili.
Wikaaila, longoli kukesale nekakunlongeela, sunga mukumiona ndogwe etungilwe palungwanso, nung'wa ndogwa palung'wi nuyo. Itungueli nukuileta kung'waane.
Anga muntu wihi wamuila kehi kua nelanso, mukulunga, 'Mukulu uitakile,' numuntu nuanso ukukaya kumugimbwa mize palung'wi nizo.
Ikani nelanso inge ilo naelekeiye kuanyahedagu kusinja ligeelekele. Wikaaila.
Aeli iana akisungu akasayuni, egoza, umutimi wako upembilye kung'waanyu, mupolo hange unaulie mundogwe, nung'wa ndogwe mugoha, ng'wa ndogwe mudabu.
Hange iamanyisigwa ekalongola ekituma anga u Yesu naualagiiye.
Ikamualeta undogwe nu ng'waa ndogwe, nukueka iang'wenda migulyaao, nu Yesu wikikie nung'wanso.
Iidu mumilundo ekaila iangwenda ao munzila niauye ehatema imatambi kupuma mumahota nukaile munzila.
Iumbi naelemutongee u Yesu nawa naiamulyatile iha hulya mduli, nukulunga, ''Hosana kung'wana wang'wa Daudi! Ukembelilwe uzile kulima lamukulu; Hosana migulwa kukila.
U Yesu paekapika kuYelusalemu, kesale kehi kekitumba nukulunga, ''Uyu nyenyu?
Iumbe lekalunga, ''Uyu Yesu munyakidagu, kupuma kunazaleti akuGalilaya.
Hange u Yesu wekingela mitekeelo ( ang'wi Tunda. Akaazunsa ehi hunzi naiakugulya nukugula mitekeelo. Wekapeula ga numeza neyaantu nae akukaila impia ne maintu naagulya nkume.
Wikaaila, ''Iandekile, ''Ito lane lekutula ito nelakulompela, kuite unyenye mametenda ikulungu laii.
Hange iapulu nea kilele ika miziila mitekeelo, nung'wenso wikaakomya.
Kuite kumatungo eakulu amakuhani neaandeki naiaine imakula naumiyumi, hange naeigule iang'enya ahuzugalya mitekeelo nukulunga, ''Hosana ng'wana wang'wa Daudi, ''ihaambwa makuo.
Ikamuila, ''Wigulene nehe kulambulwa neantu awa? U Yesu wikaaila, ''Ee! kuite muikele kusoma, kupuma mumelomo ang'enya neadabu neakankamukete likimo lupikile.
Hange u Yesu wikaaleka nuikulongola kunzi nakisale mu Bethania nukulala kuko.
Ikedaudau nausukile mukesali, aeukete nzala.
Wikaleona ikota mumpelompelo anzila. Wikalehanga, kuite shanga wikalya angakentu, mung'wanso inge ematutu du. Akauele, Itule tile inkali kung'waako lukulu hange. ''Hange itungu lelo imtini wekuma
Amanyisigwa akwe naiaine, ikakulwa nukulunga, yatuleka ule umtini wuma nkua eng'wi?
U Yesu wikasusha nukulunga, ''Tai kumuila, ang'wi mihutula nuuhueli muleke kuailya, shanga mukituma eke nekitumilwe kumtini udu, kuite mukuuila ate ulugulu, uholwe ugung'we mubahali, yukutula.
Kehi nemukulompa kusola, kunu eze muhuie mukusengiilya.
U Yesu naupikile mutekeelo, akulu amakuhane anyampala antu ekamuhanga imalungo naukumanyisa nukukolya, kuuhumi ke ukituma imakani aya? Hange nyenyu nukupee uhumi uwu?
U Yesu wihasusha nukuaila, nunene hange kumukolya ikolyo nen'wi. Ang'wi mukumbila, nunene uu kumuila kuuhumi ke nekituma imakani aya.
Ubadisigwa nuang'wa Yohana aeupumile pee, kulumdane ang'wi kuantu? Ikiholya ienso, akalunga, anga kulunge, aeupumile kilunde ukuuila, nehe mukahita kuhuila?
Kuite anga kulunge, aeupumile kuantu, ''kogopile imaumbie, kunsoko ehi aine uYohana kena munyakedagu.''
Hange ekasusha kung'wa Yesu nukulunga, ''Shakuine'' Nung'wenso wikaaila gwa, ''Nunene singa kumuila kuushumi he kituma emakani aya.
Kuite mukusinga ntuni? Umuntu nukete iama abiili Wikenda kung'wi nukumuila, Ng'waane, longola witume umulemo mumugunda nuamezabebu.
Lelo, ''Ung'wana wikasusha nukulunga, shaninzuu, kuite panyambele wikakaila imasigo akwe nukulongola.
Nu muntu nuanso wikalongola kung'wana nuanso akasusha nukulunga ninzuu, Mukulu, huite shanga wekenda.
Nuule kuawa neabiili nuilumile anga nuTata wakwe nauloilwe? Ikalunga, ''Ng'wana nuangwandyo'' U Yesu wikaaila, ''Itai kumuila, iamanangwa neakosi ahingela muutemi wang'wi Tunda kuleka hanza unyenye hingela.
Kundogoilyo u Yohana auzile kitalanyu kunzila nenguloku, kuite singa meka muhuela, mutungo ia manangwa nea kosi akamuhuela. Nu nyenye naimuine nelanso lekole, shanga mekaungana nsoko mieka mumuluile.
Tegeeli ikilingasiilo nekiuya, aukule muntu, umuntu aukele ieneo ikulu nelihi. Auteme imizabibu, unkakitiila, wikazipya nihiseme nekakukamula imagai, akazenga numuhala nualindi nukuliliha kuagaza zabibu. Hange wekenda kehengiza.
Imatungu amaogola amizabibu naeuhugee, wikaatuma atuungwa ang'wi, Umuya ekamubulega, nu muya ung'wi ikamukua namagwe.
Kuite awe neelima izabibu ikazihola eihimi akwe, ihamuhua ung'wi, Umuiye eka mubalaga, nu muya ung'wi ikamukua namagwe.
Kumkua nengiza, umugole wikaatuma atungwi angiza, eeelu kukila awa neangwandyo, huite awa neelima akaaleda hange wudu.
Nai akahila nanso umuhulu nuanso akamutuma latalao uug'waalawe nukulunga, ahumukulyaumngwane.
Kuite awa neelma emezabibu naeamwine umuhumba nuanso, Akiela, Uyu musali, Nzii, kumbulage nukuhola uusali.
Uu ekamuhola, ekamugume kunzi na mugunda nua mizabibu nukumubulaga.
Itee umukola mugunda nua mizabibu nuzile, utenda uli ialemi amezabibu?
Ikamuila, ''Ukuabipya iantu nuanso abi kunzila aulaki kukila, ne hange ukusalisha umugunda nua mizabibu kulumiangeza, iantu neahuli pa kunzila amezabibu neakahonda''.
U Yesu wikaaila '' Shamusomilene numaandeko,' Igwe nealatulile iaashi naina igwa ikulu nelaukundeki, Ile lepumile kumukulu, hange ukuleta ikuilwa kumiho iluu?
Uu kumuila, Utemi wang'wi Tunda ukuholwa kupuma kitalanyu nukupegwa ihe nekee inkali yalawe.
Wehi nuekagwa nugwe nelanso ukubungwa ninoo. Kuite kuehi nelelumugwila, lekumusia.
Ikulu amakuhani nea mafalisayo naeakija ilingasilyo yakwe, ikaona kena akulambulwa enso.
Kuite kela naealoilwe kugoola mikono migulya lakwe, akagopa umilundo, kunsoko iantu aeamugozile anga munyakidagu.
U Yesu autambue neenso mulengasiilyo nukulunga.
'''Utemi wa kilunde wumpyani numutemi naoneneeye wiloelinua winga wang'waakwe.
Wikaatuma eitumi akwe husila awa neaalehikweize muwiloeli nua winga, huite sengaikapika.
Umutemi wikaatuma hange eitumi angizawikalunga. ''Aeli ehe neanilwe, Gozi, nanonelyaindya. Nakwa neamudama neaginu asinzwaa, ne makani ehi ahondilile, Nzii hiloelye muwinga''.
Kuite iantu awa singaai akee lukulu uamwi wakwe. Neang'wi ikalongola kumigunda ao, nawa niangiza ikalongola mumaanza ao nabiashala.
Niangiza ikaaja eitumi amukulu nukuabulaga.
Kuite umutemi wikataka. Wikatuma ikua mbiteakwe akabulangwa eabulagi nukulimansiilya ikisalekao kumoto.
Hange wikaaila eitumi akwe, ''Uwinga ukondile, kuite ianwi shangaaza.
Kuitelongoli muninsambwa nzile nemehulu, muane iantu needu anga uu neukuhuma aze muwiloeli nua winga.''
Eitumi akena munzila ninkulu nukuakalibisha iantu ehi nae aine, aza kuabi, Uu itando nila winga ieizula iageni.
Kuite umutemi nae wingie nukuagoza iaiziila, wikamuona muntu ung'wi akeze mugila ung'wenda nua winga.
Umutemi akamukolya, Muhumba miane, azaupikile ule apakunu umugila ung'we nua winga? Numuntu nuanso shanga wikasushaketi.
Uu gwa umutemi akaaila eitumi akwe, Mutungi umuintu uyu imekono nemegulu mugumi kunzi kuhiti, kung'wanso nuuhole uleli nukusia muno.
Kunsoko antu edu itangilwe, kuite awa niasaguwe ashenyu.
Uu iatalisayu ikahega nukuzipeilya amurambe uyehu munkani yakwe ung'wenso.
Uuikaatuma iamanyisigwa ao palung'wi Helode Hange ikamuila uYesu, ''Mumanyisi, kulengile kenauewe wimuntu watai, hange kena ukumanyisa ita ang'wi Tunda etai shanga ukee mkani ningiza hange umugila anga ukweli nua antu.
Kuite kuile, usegile ntuni? Itee? taine kilago kapunya ehodi nshenyu ang'wi alii?
U Yesu aulengile uubi wao wikalunga, Kuneki nemungema unye nemiamasue?
Ndangiili empia netumeka mukodi.''Uu ikamutetela edinali.
U Yesu akakolya ''Ikelu ne lina ele lang'wi nyanyu?
Ikasusha,''Yang'wa kaisari.'' Uu Yesu akabila,''Mupiukaisari nakwe nang'wi Tunda mupi Itunda.''
Naeigule ile ikakuilwa. Hange ikamuleka nukulongola yao.
Iluhiku nulanso ang'wi ao amasadukayo akiza kung'wa Yesu, awa neelunga kutile anga uiukiwaashi. Ekamukulya,
akalunga,''Mumanyisi, Umusa aulugile, Angeze umuntu ukule singa utugile ung'wana, umuluna ukumusala umusungu nuanso nukumuligelya ung'wana nsoko amuluna wakwe.
Aeahote atuna mupungate. Nua ng'wandyo autenile wikasha shuutungile ung'wana. Aka mutekela umulune umusungu.
Hange umulune wakwe wikalenda uu, hange nuyu nuaka taatu, yekatenda uu sunga yuyu nua mupungate.
Nae ituma ite ehi, numusungu nuanso wikasha.
Inge muuiuki umusungu nuanso ukutula wang'wanyenyu mualuna neanso nemupungate? kunsoko ehi ae amutenile.''
Kuite u Yesu ausuhilye nukulunga, Mukakoseela, Kunsoko shamumanyile Imaandeko sunga ningulu niang'wi Tunda.
Kunsoko muuniuhi, iantu shaitena ang'wi hulenwa, kuleka ite iantu etula anga iamakika hilunde.
Kuite uiuki waashi mukele musomene niTunda auketambue kitalanyu, nukulunga.
Unene ni Tunda nuang'wa Iblahimu, Itunda wang'wa Isaki, ni Tunda nuang'waYakobo? Itunda singa Itundawaashi, inge Itunda nua panga.''
Imatungo umulundo nuahija ile, ikakuilwa umanyisi wakwe.
Kuite emafalisayo niakija kena Uyesu wakilaja ea masadukayo, ekiiligeila ienso palug'wi.
Ung'wiao, akeze munyilago, wika mukolya ikolyokumugema.
Mumanyisi, ilago neleuke ni kulu kukele imalago ehi.
U Yesu akasusha,''kusinja umulowe umukulu kunholo ako ehi, nemahala ako ehi.
Ili lilo ilagilyo ikulu hangi nilang'wandyo.
Hange na akabiili impyani ni yiyo. Kusinja kumulowa u munya kisali anga nuiloilwe u ewe.
Imalago ehi neanya kidagu imeiwe nemalago yaya nabiili.
Ne mafalisayo naekili ilingile paluug'wi, U Yesu akaakulya ikolyo.
Akalunga,''Itee? Musegile ntuni kung'wa Kristo? Nuanso ng'wa nyenyu? Neenso ekasusha,'' Ng'wana wang'wa Daudi.
U Yesu wikaasukeelya.''Kuuhuni kea udaudi ike ni nkolo ukumitanga mukulu, nukulunga.
Mukulu auumuie Umukulu wane,'' Ikieumohono wanenuakegohe, sunga nekuatenda ialugu aho aikwepihe amegulu aho?''
Ang'wi Udaudi ukumitanga ukristo,''Mukulu''Ukutulang'waakwe ule?
Kutile nae usuhilye ulukani hanga, hange hutile naugemile kumukolya imakolyo nendu kupuma uluhiku lulo nukulongoleka.
Kuleka ite auligilye ne antu neamanyisigwa ahwe,
''Iaandeki neamafalisayo ikaie ituntu lang'wa Musa.
Kehi neakumuila kituma, itumi kunu mezeagoza. Kuita muteke kituma intendo yao, kunsoko neanso elunga imakani neshaituma.
Itai etunga meligo melito neanso hange mekaku humehenha, hange eahensha iantu mumeenga ao. Kuite neanso shaehugeela ata ninino kukenha.
Inlendo yao yehi, ituma nsoko agozwe neantu. Kunsoko neanso igalipya imasandeko ao nukongeelya ukuulu nua upendi wang'wenda ao.
Neanso ilowa kikie muianza yakikulya muumalagone mumatuntu akakulya mukate amumasinagogi,
nuhulamushigwa kukulyo nkani yakusoko, nukulang'wa, ''Amanyisi'' ne antu.
Kuite unye singainonee kitangwa''Miamanyisi'' Kunsoko muukete umumanyisi ung'wi, hange unye meehi mekiluna.
Muleke kuuitanga muntu wehi apa mihe kena Tata wanyu, kunsoko mukete Tata wang'wi alua, nung'wenso ukole hilunde.
Hange muleke kitangwa ''amanyisi'' kunsoko mukete umumanyisi ung'wi duu, inge Kristo.
Inge numukulu mulalanyu ukutala mutumi wanyu.
Wehi nukihumbula ukusimigwa, hange wehi nukisimya ukuhumbulwa.
Kuite ukea wanyu aandeki nea mafalisayo, ateele! mukua lugaile iantu utemi nuakilunde. Nunyenyeshamuhumile kingela, shamuagombilye neakingela hutende ite.

Ukae wanyu aandeki neafalisayo, ateele! Mukuputa itumbe labahali nukumutenda umuntu ung'wi wahuele kuaya nemukumanyisa. hangi nuekatenda anga unyenye, mukumulenda kabiili muntu nue [kumoto] jehanamu anga uu uuyenye nemile.
Ukae wanyu atongeeli nea poku, unye nemilunga, wehi nuelapa kitekeelo, singa kentu. Kuite nuelapa kilapo la zahabu ni lekeelo, ukulungwa nekelapokakwe.
Unye apoku meapungu, nekeule nekekulu kukelakeuya, zahabune angwi itekeelo neliikilwe wakufu nezahabu kung'wi Tunda?
Hange, wehi nukulapa kuzahabu, singa kentu. Inge nukulapa kisongelyo nelekole mung'waakwe, utungilwa nuulapi wakwe.
Unye antu nemeapoku, nekeule nekekulu kukele ikiunya isongeelyona ang'wi adhabu neekwa wakufu imasongeilyo nepumigwa kung'wi Tunda?
Kuite, nuanso nuelopa kuzahabu wilapa kunelanso nukumaintu ehe nahole kung'wa akwe.
Nung'wenso nuelapa mitekeelo, wilapa kunelanso kung'wenso nuekili akwe.
Nung'wenso nuelapa kiluunde, wilapa pituntu la utemi ne lang'wi Tunda nukung'wenso nuikie mung'wanso.
Ukae wanyu, aandeki neafalisayo, ateele! kunsoko mukupunya ezaka kubizali, mnaanaa nechicha, kuita mukuleka imakani nemalito milego -tai ukende, nuuhueli. Kuite aya yemunonee kutula mutumile, hange singa kumaleka nemangiza muhile kumitumela.
Unye atongeeli nemeapoku, nemukusuza umududu numuniino kuite mukuimela ingamia!
Ukae wanyu, andeki neafalisayo, miateele! Kunsoko mukoja ikole kunzi ne sahani kuhunzi, kuite kunzi izue uubi hange kulile anga upolo.
Unye aaafalisa nemiapoku, oji hanza ikole mukati ne mukati a sahani, nsoko inkika na kunzi etule nza nenyenso gaa.
Ukae wanyi, aandeke neafalisayo, meateele! kunsoko mukimpyana niibeela napakilwe ukenke, kunzi igela maza, kuite mukati izue imakupa naashi hange kela kentu neke bii.
Uulukuli, nunye kunzi migee kena miaza ntongeele aantu, kuite kunzi mizue uteele nuubi.
Ukae wanyu, aandeki neafalisayo, meateele! kunsoko mukuzenga iibiila na anyakidagu nukupambe iibiila yao awa nea tai.
Unye milunga, anga aekikie mumahiku a tata itu, shanga aezekipalung'wi nao kuhunula usakami nuanya kidagu.
Kuite mukihenga unyenye kena unye miana ao awa nae abulagile ianyakidagu.
Hange unyenye mukupikeelya kizulya pang'wanso niinonee umulandu nua Tata anyu.
Unye nzoka, akete vipilibao, muuekile ule uulamuli nuakujehanamu?
Kuite, goza, kuatuma kitalanyu ianyakidagu, antuneakuligwa, neaandeki, Ang'wi ao mukuabulaga nukuaja. Ang'wiao mukuakua mumasinagogi anyu nukuazunsa nukupuma makesale king'wi sunga numuya.
Upumeli kena kung'wa anyu ukupumela usakami wehi nua tai nauhunuwe mihe, kaziilya isakamiang'wa Habili nua tai sunga isakani niya Zakalia ung'waa Balaki, nae mumubulabile patakatifu nepa kezindaalo.
Tai, kumuila, imakani aya ehi akuupata uwileli uwu.
Yerusalemu, Yerusalemu, uewe nukeze abulaga ianyakidagu nukuakua namagwe awa neatumilwe kung'wa ako! Nkua inga kumilingeela iang'enya ako palung'wi anga enkuku nilingeela iana akwe mumanana akwe, kuite singa wikagomba!
Goza ito lako lasaga nuula.
Nunee kuila, kandeelya, itungo lele nukulongoleka singa umona, sunga nuekalunga, “Ukembetilwe nuanso nuzile kulina nela Mukulu.”
U Yesu akapuma mitekeelo akalongola kwea. Iamanyisigwa akwe ikamuhanga nukumulagiila imajengo amatekeelo.
Kuite akasusha nukuaila, “Itee, shamuine ne imakani aya ehi? Itai kumuila, kutile igwe nelekusaga migulya alulya nesha nukuhambulwa.”
Hange pawikikie mulugulu nula Mizeituni, iamanyisigwa akwe ekamuhanga akeze ipihie nukulunga, “Kuite imakani aya akupumela nale? Kentu ke nekikutula kelingasiilyo kakuza kung'waako ne mpelo aunkumbigulu?
U Yesu akasusha nukuaila, “Tuli nuugozi kena aleke umuntu kuakongela.
Kunsoko edu azile kulina lane. Akulunga, “Unene inge nene ne Kilisto, hange akuakonga edu.
Muukija mbita ni mpola nia mbita. Gozi muleke kutula nuwoa, kunsoko imakani akupumela, kuite empelo ika ikeli.
Kunsoko ihe ikauka kihe nzuya, nuutemi kuutemi uuya. Yukutula nenzala nematetemeko amahimuianza niakuli kuli.
Kuite imakani aya ehi ng'wandyo udu wauai nuakutuga.
Uu akumupumya kunsoko magigwe nukubulagwa. Mukubipilwa ne mahi ehi nsoko alina lane.
Uu edu akukumpa nukilekeelya nukibepilwe unyenye kua nyenye.
Anyakidagu edu akupumela nukuakongela edu.
Kunsoko uubi ukongeeleka, ulowa nuantu du ukupola.
Kuite uyu nukigigimiilya sunga empelo, ukuguneka.
Izi inkani nenziza nia utemi yukutanatigwa unkumbigulu wehi kutula wihengi kumahi ehi. Uu empelo ekapika.
Kuite nemekaona uwibulugi nuubi, naeletambuwa numunya kedagu u Danieli lemekile pakianza neketakatifu (nukusoma nualinge),
uu awa neakole ku Yuda amankiile mumalugulu.
Nuyu nuakole migulya mumalo waleke kusima pihe kuhola kentu keke kupuma munyumba akwe,
nuyu nuakole kumugunda aleke kusuka kuhola ung'wenda wakwe.
Kuite ukia wao neakete ung'wana nawe neakonsha mumahiku nanso!
Lompi kena kumanka kung'waanyu ileke kutula matungo ampepo, ang'wi luhiku nula kusupya.
Kunso ikalukole lwago lukulu, neze lukile lupumile kupuma kuumbwa uukumbigulu sunga nitungo gaa, singalezezigela hange.
Anga imahiku nanso anga ae akugempigwe, kutile naeweze guneka. Kuite nsoko aasagulwa, imahiku nanso akukugempigwa.
Hange angeze muntu wehi ukumuila, “Goza, Kilisto ukole papa! Ang'wi, Ukilisto ukole uko muleke kuhuila inkani nianso.
Kunsoko i Makilisto nauteele neanya kidagu auteele azile nukigeelya makula makulu naukuelwi, kunsoko akukongela, ang'wi yukuwezekana ata iasagulwa.
Gozi, namuhugula nakele kupumela.
Kuite, anga amuila, “Ukilisto ukole kumbuga, muleke kenda kung'wanso kumbuga. Ang'wi, “Gozi, ukole munyumba muleke kuhuela inkani nianso.
Anga uu nulumelika kupuma kilya nukumelika kung'weli, uu yeekatula keza kung'wana nuang'wa Adamu.
Pehi nuukole umuimba, kung'wanso kuko indeeyilingeela.
Kuite matungo makupe kukela yekatula nulwago lukulu imahiku nanso, Ilya lukuikilwa kiti, ung'weli shaukupumya uwelu wakwe, inzota yukugwa kupuma kilunde, ningulu yakilunde yukuhingieka.
Uu ekelingasiilyo ka ng'wana wang'wa Adamu ekigela migulya, ni ntambu yehi ni amihe yako hongelya. Akumuona ung'wana nuang'wa Adamu upembilye mumalunde amigulya kungulu nuukulu nukulu.
Ukuatuma iamalaika akwe kululi nulukulu alalumbeta, neensa akuulingiila palung'wi iasagulwa akwe kupuma nande ine nia mihe, kupuma mpelo ung'wini lunde sunga neye nengiza.
Imanyisi isomo kupuma mumtini. Anga itambee liketegela nukupumya imatutu, malenga kena iketiku kahugeela.
Uu gwa, anga maona imakani aya ehi, mulenge kena wahugeela, pakupi pamulango.
Itai kumuila, uwitugi uwu shaukukila, sunga imakani aya igele.
Ilunde nihi yukukela, kuite inkani yane shayukukila kwee.
Kuile kuluhiku nulanso nesasa kutile umuntu nuine, ata umalaika nua kilunde, ang'wi ung'wana, inge u Tata ung'wana wang'wenso udu.
Anga uu naeyeli mumatungo ang'wa Nuhu, uu yukutula keza kung'wana wang'wa Adamu.
Kunsoko mumahiku nanso imazi naeakeli kigela iantu ae akulya nukung'wa, akutina nukutinwa kupika uluhiku lulo nu Nuhu aewingile musafina,
hange shanga aealingile kentu kehi sunga emazi nai ahangile nukuchola ehi uu yukutula heza kung'wana wang'wa Adamu.
Uu antu abiile ika akole kumugunda, ung'wi ukuholwa, ung'wi ukulekwa kunyuma.
Asungu abiili ikaa eze sia palung'wi, ung'wi ukuholwa, ung'wi ukusaga.
Kuite, tuli meahugu nsoko shamuine luhiku ke nuzile u Mukulu wanyu.
Kuite mulenge kena, angeze umukulu nuito angize azuine itungo ke nuzile umuhembi, azuzekesha shanga azuzee leka ito lakwe kubunangwa.
Kuite, inonee gwa mutule mukondile, kunsoko ung'wana wang'wa Adamu uzile itungo nesungamuine.
Ite nyenyu numulindie, mutugwa nukele imakala, umukulu wakwe umupee uuhumi kuawa neakole nuto lakwe, nsoko waape indya kumatungo nanonee?
Ukembetilwe umitumi nuanso, u Mukulu wakwe ukumuhanga ukitume uu imatungo nuzile.
Itai kumuila kena umukulu ukumuika mukela kentu nekakwe.
Kuite umutugwa ang'wi mubii ukulunga munkolo akwe, “Mukulu wane watinia,”
wandye kuakua eitumi akwe, hange wang'we nukulya palung'wi nuhugala.
U Mukulu nua mutugwa nuanso uzile uluhiku numugila ata isigo, numitungu nushuine.
U Mukulu wakwe ukumutema ipande ibiili nukumuika mulyoma ling'wi anga asambo, kung'wanso ikole kulila nukusia emino.
Uu utemi wakilunde ukipyanigwa neawali nikuminaahole intala yao ekalongola kumupokela ubwana nuawinga.
Antaano ao ae apungu nawa neangiza ataano aeaelewa.
Eanawali neapungu ekahola intala yao, shanga ekahola emakuta.
Hange aenawali awa neaelewa ekahola iseme yao nemakuta palungwi ni ntala yao.
Imatungo yayo Ubwana nuawinga naushelewe kupika, ehi akahung'wa tolo ekalala.
Lakini utiku wakatekate akakakuta ngwano,''Goza, ubwana nuawinga! Pumi kunzi mumusingeelye.
Uu neenso enawali ehi akauka ekakakelya intala yao.
Awa neapunga ekaaela awa neelewa, 'Mukongelye esehemu amakuta anyu kunsoko intala yitu yukulima.'
Lakini awa neaelewa ekaasukilya ekaaela, 'Kunsoko shanga akutosilye unyenye nusese, kuite longoli kwa awaneegulya miguelye ekeasi kanyu nekemutosilye.
Imatungo naalongoe neanso kugula, Ubwana wawinga wekapika, ne matungo naakole tayali aeendile nang'wenso kushelehe awinga, numulango wikalugailwa.
Baadae enawali neangiza naapikile ekalunga, ''Bwana, bwana, kulungwile.''
Lakini akaasukelya nukulunga,'Etai kumuela, shanga numumanyile.
Kuite gozi, kunsoko shangamuihe ematungo luhiku ang'wi saa.
Kuite sawa numuntu nautakile kusafili kulongola ihe ngeza aeutangile eatugwa akwe nukuapa ugole wakwe.
Ung'wiao wekamupa talanta itaano, uyu numungiza wekamupa ibeele, nuyuite wekamupa eng'wi. Kela ung'wiao aupokee kiasi kulengana nuuwezo wakwe, numuntu nuanso weka safili kulongola yakwe.
Mapema uyu naupokee entalanta niitano wikalogola wekaelya, nukutugisa talanta itaano hange.
Uu uu nuyu naeupokee italanta nibeele, aeutugizilye ni nzuya ibeele.
Lakini umutugwa naeupokee talanta eng'wi, wikalongola yakwe wikahemba ishimu pihe, ite wikamepiha empia ang'wa bwana akwe.
Na baada matungo malepu, Ubwana watungwa neanso wekasuka nukuzepelya emaesabu neenso.
Umutugwa nuanso nausengeeye italanta niitano auzile wikaleta ningeeza itaano. wikalunga, Bwana, azumpee talanta iitano. Goza napata efaeda atalanta ngiza itaano.
Ubwana akwe wikamuila,'' Hongera, mutugwa numuza nuuhueli! Umuhueli kuintu niino. Kuupa emadalaka migulya kuintu niidu. Ingele muiloelyi wang'wa Bwana ako.
Umutugwa nausengeye italanta niibeele wekeza nukulunga, Bwana, aumpee talanta ibeele. Goza napata faeda atalanta geza ibeele.
Ubwana akwe wekamuela,''Hongeeli mutugwa numuza nuuhueli kumaintu nemakehu. Kuupa emadalaka migulya kumaintu needu. Ingile wiloelye mung'wa Bwana ako.''
Baadae umutugwa naupokee etalanta neng'we aewezie wekalunga,''Bwana, nengile kina uewe umuntu mutaki wevuna pang'wanso neshanga uhusekile.
Unene nekogopa, nekenda yane nekapiha etalanta akopihe. Goza, ukete hapa nekako.''
Lakini ubwana wikamusukilya wekalunga. 'Uewe umutugwa mubee, aulengile kina nekala pang'wanso neshanga ntemee nukuvuna pang'wanso neshanganihusekile.
Kuite aeizepie kuapa empia ane entu abenki, nematungo naensukile kung'wane aezemesengelya nane palung'wi nefaeda.
Apa muhegelyi etalanta nanso mumupe utugwa nukete talanta nikumi.
Kila umuntu nukete nekakwe, okongeligwa ikulu ata ukuzidisheligwa. Lakini kwa uyu nemugila ekentu, ga nekenukete ukuhegeligwa.
Mugumi kunzi kukiti umutugwa nuanso neshanga ufaile hange ikutula kelelo nukukelya emino!
Ematungo ung'wa Adamu nuekeza nuutukufu wakwe, naealaeka ehi palung'wi nung'wenso, Uu ukikie migulya ituntu lakwe nuutukufu.
Indugu yehi ikilingeela ntongeela akwe, nung'wenso ukuabagala eantu. Anga umudemi nuebagula inkolo nimbuli.
Ukuieka inkolo mukono wakwe nuwakigoha, ite ukiekaimbuli mokono wankege.
Ite umufalme ukuaela awa nea mukono wakegoha, Nzii, nemukembetilwe nu Tata anyi, usali ufalme nauandalewe kunsoko anyu kupuma ukuekwa emesingi au nkumbigulu.
Hange aenkete nzala mekampa indya; Ae nemugeni mukankalibisha.
Ae nkole kepwe, mekantugala eang'wenda; Ae numulwae mekantunza; Ae nkole muketungo mukangoza!
Uu awa neatai akumusukelya nukumuela, Bwana, Nale aekukuine ukete nzala kekakulesa? Ang'wi ukete nyota kekakupe maze? Hange nale nae kukuine umugeni kekaku kalibisha? Ag'wi ukete nyota kekakupa emaze?
Ang'wi nale naekukuine umugeni nakekakukalibesha? Hange umugila anga lang, wenda kekakutugala eang'wenda?
Ang'wi nale naeumulwae, ang'wi ukole muketungo kekeza kuugoza?
Na umufalme ukuasukelya, etai kumuela, naemutendile apaite kung'wi anyandugu ane neanino, aemuntendee nene!
Kuite ukuaela awa neakole umukono wakwe nuankege; Hegi kitalane unye nemukete emasatiko, Longoli kumoto nua kulenakale naeuandalewe kunsoko ang'wa shetani neamalaeka akwe;
Kunsoko aenkete nzala shanga mekakumpa indya; Ae nkete nyota shanga kekakupa emaze;
Ae nemugeni shanga mekankalibisha; Ae nkolekepwe shanga mekampa eang'wenda; Ae nemulwae ae ntungilwe kuite shanga mekangoza.
Au nawa neanso aku musukelwa nukulunga, Bwana nale naekukuine ukete nzala ang'wi nyota, ang'wi umugeni, ang'wi ukepwe ang'wi umulwae, ang'wiutungilwe, shanga kekakuhudumela?
Ite ukuasukelya nukulunga,''Etai kumuela, eke neshanga aemuatendee awa neanino, shangaae muntendee anga nene.
Awaite inzu kuazabu akale nakale kuite awa neatai upanga wakale na kale.''
Imatungo u Yesu naumaile kutambula inkani yehi niyanso, akaaela eamanyisigwa akwe,
“Mulengile kina baada amahiku abeele kuutula nesikukuu, nung'wana wang'wa Adamu ukupumigwa kuite wasulubiwe.”
Baadaye eakulu amakuhani neanyampala neantu aeatankanile palung'wi pakate pamakao ang'wa kuhani numukulu, naewitangwa Kayafa.
Kwa palung'wi ekupanga enjama akumuamba u Yesu kwa unkunku nukumubulaga.
Kunsoko aalungile, “Ileke kutula matungo asikukuu, kuite ilekekuleta eghasia pakatekate aantu.”
Imatungo u Yesu naukole ku Bethania munyumba ang'wa Simoni umukoma,
naukole ukionyesha pameza, musungu ung'wi aewezile kitalakwe aukenkile mukebe nuwa alabasta naekete imakukuta naake ethama nkulu, na aeumahunuie migulya mitwe lakwe.
Lakini eamanyisigwa akwe naaine ikani eleite, aabepewa nukulunga, “Kunsokoke easala eyeite?
Ayaite ahumekile aguligwe kukeasi kekolo nukupegwa eaula.”
Lakini u Yesu kunsoko aaulengile eleite, wekaaela. “Kuneke mukumusumbula umusungu uyuite? Witumile kentu kezakung'wane.
Eaula mukete mahiku ehi, lakini shangamukutula mukole nunene mahiku ehi.
Kunsoko nauhunue imakuta mitwe lane aya migulya wa mwele wane, aewitumile ite kunsoko ukuekwa kung'wane.
Kutai kumuela, pehi ulukani ulu nulekatambulwa pakate aunkumbigulu wehi, eketendo nukitumile umusungu uyuite, hange kekutambulwa kunsoko akumbukumbu.”
Kuite ung'wiao nua awa nekumi nambele, naewitangwa Yuda Iskariote, akenda kwa akulu amakuhani,
nukulunga “Mukumpa ntuni anganumusaliti?” Akamupimela u Yuda ipande thelathini niyampia.
Hange imatungo yayo wekaduma enafasi akumusaliti.
Hata uluhiku lang'wando nuamekate neshanga eekewe igae, eamanyisigwa akwe aeendile kung'wa Yesu nukulunga, Pe nutakile kukuandaelye ulye indya ya Pasaka?”
Wekaaela, Longoli kumujini kumuntu fulani namueli, Ung'walimu ukulunga, “Ematungo ane ahumbeela kumetimelya epasaka palung'wi neamanyisigwa ane, pakate panyumbako.”
Emanyisigwa akituma anga u Yesu naualageye, na andae indya ya Pasaka.
Naeipikile mpende, aewikie kulya indya palung'wi neamanyigwa kumi nambeele.
Naakulya indya, wikalunga, “Etai kumuela ung'wi anyu ukunisaliti.”
Ekapyenenkela kule, kila ung'wiao akandya kumukolya, “Ite shanganene Mukulu?”
Akaasukilya, “Uyu nukutala umukono wakwe palung'wi nunene mukate mibakuli yuyo ukunisaliti.
Ung'wana wang'wa Adamu ukuhega, anga naeyandekilwe. Lakini isateko lakwe umuntu nuekamusaliti ung'wana wang'wa Adamu! Azetula tazu kumuntu nuanso angae waleke kutugwa.”
U Yuda, nae uzemusaliti wikalunga, ite nene Labi? U Yesu wekamuila, “Ukutambula ulukani nulanso uewe.”
Naatuile ukulya indya, u Yesu wikauhola umukate, akaukembeta, nukuega. Wikaapa eamanyisigwa akwe nukulunga, “Holi, mulye. Uwu wuwu mweele waane.”
Wekahola ekekombe nukukembeta, akaapa nukulunga, “Wing'wi mehi kuekeite.
Kunsoko uyu sakami wane nuilago lane, nekuhunulwa kwa ehi kumusamaha waanyamendu.
Lakini kumuela, shangakung'wa hange inkali yamezabibu uwaie, hadi uluhiku ulo nenzeng'wa nepya palung'wi nunyenye pakate autemi wang'wa Tata ane.”
Nakondilye kemba uwembo, ekapuma ekalongola kumulema wa Mizeituni.
Hange u Yesu wikaaela, “Utiku wuwu mehi mukukumpa kunso ane, kunsoko yandekilwe, kumukua umudemi wikundi lankolo ninyenso ikusambaela.
Lakini baada akuiuka kung'wane, kumutongela kulongola ku Galilaya.”
Lakini u Petelo wikamuila, “Hata anga ehi akuhite kunsoko amakani nakuhanga, nakuupata, unene shanga kuhita.
U Yesu wikamusukelya, “Etai kuela, utiku wuwu kabla ujogoo wakunkule, ukunihita nkua itaatu.”
U Petelo wikamuela, “hata kina impasile kusha nuewe, singa kuuhita.” Neamanyisigwa neangeza ehi ekalunga uu, uu.
Baadaye u Yesu wikalongola neenso pang'wenso niitangwa Gethsemane nawikaaela eamanyisigwa akwe, “Ikie hapa ematungo neninzu uko kulompa.”
Akamuhola u Petelo neana abeele neang'wa Zebedayo na wikandya kupyenenkela nukusononeka.
Hange wikaaela, “Enkolone ekete kenyauwai kekulu kule ata ekeasi kakusha. Sagi hapa mukeshe palung'wi nunene.”
Wekalongola kuntongela inino, wikagwa kifudifudi, nukulompa. Wikalunga, “Tata ane, peza iwezekanile, ekekombe ekeite kenkwepe. Iteke kutula anga nentakile unene, hange kina nutakile uewe.”
Akaahanga eamanyisigwa wekaahanga alala tulo, kunso emiho aemalito.
Keshi nukulompa kunso mulekekingila mumagemo. Inkolo akole radhi, lakini umweele udhaifu.
Akalongola yakwe nkua akabeele nukulompa, akalunga, “Tata ane kina ulukani ulu shangaiwezekanile kulekwepa lazima nukeng'we ekekombe ekeite, emapenzi ako atimele.”
Wekasuka hange wikahanga alala tulo, kunsoko emiho ao ae malito.
Kuite wikaaleka hange wekalongola yakwe. Akalompa enkua akatuatu inkani zizo zizo.
Baadaye u Yesu wekaahanga eamanyisigwa akwe nukuaela, “Kele mukie ne nukusupya? Gozi ematungo ahumbeela, nung'wana wang'wa Adamu ukusalitiwa mumekono aanyamelandu.
Uki kuhege. Gozi uyuite nung'wenso nukunsaliti wahugela.”
Ematungo naukele ukuligitya, u Yuda ung'wi wa awa nenkumi na mbeele, akapika. Lulili lukulu lukapika palung'wi nung'wenso anga lepumele kwa akulu amakuhani neanyampala neantu. Ae azile nimpanga niidunkuli.
Hange umuntu naeudee kumusaliti u Yesu auapee eshala, akalunga, “Uyu nenekamulungela, ng'wenso muambi.”
Imatungo yayo wekiza kung'wa Yesu nukulunga, “Na wikamulungela.
U Yesu wikamuila, “Muhumba meane itume ele nelekutile uu akeza, nukumugoolela emekono u Yesu, nukumuamba.
Goza, muntu ung'wi naukole palung'wi nu Yesu, wikagoola umukono wakwe, wikahopola upanga wakwe, na wikamukua umitumi wang'wa kuhani numukulu, nukumuamba ukutwe wakwe.
Uu Yesu wikamuila, susha upanga wako pana aza uhoe, kunsoko ehi neetumila upanga akuangamizigwa kwa upanga.
Ite mulungile shanganihumilene kumitanga u Tata ane, nung'wenso ukuntumela emajeshi zaidi akumi na mbeele na amalaeka?
Lakini ite emaandiko awazekanile kutimeligwa, kuite uu ipasilwe kupumila?
Imatungo yayo u Yesu wikauela umilundo, “Ite mezile nemapanga neidunkuli kumamba kina uyu nuehegelanya? Kila imahiku aenikie mihekalu nukumumanyisa nashangaemumambile!
Lakini ayaite ehe itumilwe ite emaandiko anyakedagu atimile. “Uu emanyisigwa akwe ekamuleka nukumanka.
Awa naamuambile u Yesu akamutala kung'wa Kayafa, u Kuhani nu mukulu pang'wanso eaandeki neanyampala aeilingie palung'wi.
Kuite u Petelo aiumutyatile kunyuma kukuli kupikila mu itando nilang'wa Kuhani u Mukulu. Ai wingie mukate nukikie palung'wi nienso wihenga mukikapumila.
Kuite eakulu amakuhani nebalaza lehi aeakuduma ushahidi wauteele dhidi ang'wa Yesu kunsoko ahume kumubulaga.
Kuite apumie amashaidi eedu, lakini shanga ekalija anga lukani lehi. Lakini baadaye eamashahidi abeele ekapumila pantongela.
nu kulunga, “Umuntu uyu aulungile, “Mbezile kuunanga ihekalu lang'wi Tunda nukulezenga kwa mahiku atatu.”
Ukuhani numukulu akimeka wikamukolya, “Shanga uhumilene kusukilya?
Lakini u Yesu aewikie ukilagilye ihetwe. Ukuhani numukulu wikamuela, “Anga Itunda nuikie kuamulu ukuele, kang'wi uwe wi Kilisto ng'wana wa Itunda.
U Yesu wikamusukilya, “Uwe utambue ulukani nulanso. Lakini kuela kupuma itungele nukendelea ukumuona ung'wana wang'wa Adamu wikie umukono wakulela nuukete ingulu na wikeza na malunde kigulu.”
Uu gwa u Kuhani nu Mukulu wekatamulanga eng'wenda akwe nukulunga, “Wakufulu! Ite, kutakile hange ushahidi wantuni? Goza, uu wimeka ukukufulu.
Ite mukusega ntuni? Ekamusukilya nukulunga, “Ugombigwe washe.”
Hange ekamutye emate muusu nukumukua enkunde, nukumukua emakopi kumekono ao,
nukulunga, “Wewe uewe Kilisto. Nyenyu nukukuile?
Ematungo nanso u Petelo aewikie kunzi pakate aukumbi numitumi nuakesungu wikamuhenga nukulunga, Newe ga aeukole palung'wi nu Yesu wa Galilaya.”
Lakini wekahita ntongeele ao ehi, wikalunga, singa nengile ekeite nemukutambula.”
Nae ulongoe kunzi amulango, umitumi mungiza nuakesungu wakamuona nukumuela naakole pang'wanso, “Umuntu uyu aliakoli nu Yesu wa Nazareti.”
Wikahita hange kwakulapa, “Unene shanga numumanyile umuntu uyuite.”
Ematungo makupe baadaye, awa naeimekile pakupe, ekameendela u Petelo nukulunga, “Kutai nuewe ga wiang'weao, kunsoko ata lafudhi ako ekuonyesha.”
Uu wikanza kuapa emasateko, “Unene shanga numumanyile umuntu uyuite” kuite ujogoo wekakunkula.
U Petelo wekakumbuka inkani nauewe nu Yesu, “Kabla ujogoo wekakunkula wakunihita nkua itatu.”
Ematungo ekedaudau naapikile, eakulu ehi neamakuhani neanyampala aantu aalie njama dhidi ang'wa Yesu ahume kumubulaga.
Aamutungile, aeamutongee, ekamupisha kung'wa Liwali Pilato.
Hange ematungo ang'wa Yuda, naeumusalitile, auinekina u Yesu wahukumilwa wikaambwa masego wekasusha epande thelathini niya mpia kwa akulu neamakuhani neanyampala.
Wikalunga, “Nituma melandu kumesaliti usakami nengila anga mulandu.” Lakini ekamusukelya, “Akuhusile ntuni? Magoze nanso uewe.”
Hange wikaguma pihe ipande nianso nesalani niya mpia mihekalu, wekahega yakwe wekigoga ung'wenso.
Umukulu wa Makuhani wekaihola ipande niyanso neampia nukulunga, “Singa inonene kuieka impia iziite muhazina, kunsoko agalama asakami.”
Ekikolya kwa palung'wi empia ekutumeka kuguila umugunda nelamufinyanzi nelakiieka eageni.
Kunsoko eyeite umugunda nuanso ukitangwa, “Mugunda wa sakami” ata elelo yeye.
Hange ulukani naelutambuwe numunyakedagu u Yeremia lekatimila, kulunga, “Aeatumie ipande salasini niya mpia, egalama naepangilwe neantu a Israeli kunsoko akwe,
na ae ametumie kumugunda wamufinyanzi, kina Mukulu naeundagie.”
Imatungo yayo u Yesu wekimika ntongeela ang'wa liwali nuliwali wakamukolya, “Ite uewe umutawala wa Ayahudine? U Yesu wikamusukelya, “Wewe ulungile ite.”
Lakini ematungo nae usemewe neakulu amakahani neanyampala, shanga aeusukeye lehi.
Hange u Pilato wekamuila, “Shangawigule anga mashitaka ehi kung'wako?”
Lakini singa aeumusukeye ata ulukani nulung'wi, kuite uliwali wakizula uwoa.
Kumatungo na sikukuu ae desituli aa liwali kumutungula umutungwa ung'wi nusaguwe numilundo.
Ematungo nanso aeakete mutungwa ung'wi sugu elina lakwe Balaba.
Kuite imatungo naeatuile kilundela palung'wi, u Pilato wekaakolya, “Nyenyu nemutakile kumutungule kunso anyu?” Balaba ang'wi Yesu nukitangwa Kilisto?”
Kunsoko aeuine kina amuamba kunsoko amubepewe.
Imatungo naeakoli ikie mituntu la ulamuli, umusungu wakamutumela lukani nukulunga, “Lekakituma lukani lehi kumuntu uyuite numugila anga ubee, kuite nsumbukile ikulu eleleye mundoti kunsoko akwe.”
Uu eakulu amakuhani neanyampala aashawishilye emakutano amulompe u Balaba, nu Yesu abulagwe.
U Liwali aiuwakoiye, “Nu uli kati a abiili muloilwe unene numulekele kitalanyu?” Ailigitilye “Balaba.”
U Pilato wikaaela, “Numutendele ntuni u Yesu nukitangwa Kilisto?” Ehi ekasukelya “Msulibishe.”
Nung'wenso wikalunga, “Kuneke ikosake nuitumile? Lakini aeazidilye kukulya induli yao migulya ikulu, “Musulubishe.”
Kuite imatungo u Pilato auine shangauwezilye kituma lukani lehi, lakini badalakwe efujo ekanza, wikahola emaze wekakaala emekono akwe ntongeela amilundo, nukulunga, “Unene numugila anga ubee kusakami wa muntu uyuite numugila ubee. Magozi ayaite unyenye.”
Antu ehi ekalunga, “Usakami akwe watule migulya itu neana itu.”
Hange wikamutungwila u Balaba kung'wao, lakini aeumukuile emesheleti u Yesu wekamukabidhi kung'wao alongole amusulubishe.
Hange easkale ang'wa liwali akamuhola u Yesu mpaka Praitorio numilundo nuamaskali ehi ekilundeela.
Akamutugula eang'wenda akwe nukumutugala ung'wenda nualangi nkuuku.
Hange akazepya etaji amija nukumueka migulya itwe lakwe, na amuekeye mwanzi kumukono wakwe nuakegoha. Aeakuieli imalu ao pihe ntongela akwe nukumuhonda ekalunga, “Salamu, Mutemi wa a Yahudi?”
Na amutyie emate, na aeahoile umuanzi ekamukua kitwe.
Ematungo naeakumugema, ukumutugula ung'wenda nuanso ekamutugala eang'wenda akwe, ekamulongolya kenda kumusulubisha.
Naapumile kunzi, ekamuona muntu aeupumie ku Krene elina lakwe Simeoni, hange amulazimishilye kenda nenso kuite aukenke umusalaba wakwe.
Naeapikile pang'wanso niitangwa Goligota, endogoelyo akwe ieneo li fuvu litwe.”
Amupee esiki nehangigwe nenyongo wang'we. Lakini naeumionzile, shanga wikaweza kumeng'wa.
Imatungo naamusulubishilye, ae agalanile e ang'wenda akwe kwa kuikuela kula.
Na aeikie kwa kumugoza.
Migulya mitwe lakwe aaekile mashitaka akwe ekasomeka, “Uyuite Yesu, mutemi a Wayahudi.”
Ee nyang'anyi abeele ekasulubiwa palung'we nung'wenso, ung'wi mukono wakulela ung'wi mukono wankege.
Awa naakeile ekamutanela, ekaze hingisa ematwe ao,
nukulunga, “Uewe wewe nautakile kulizepya ihekalu nukulezenga kwa nsiku itatu, iokoe uewe! Angiza wang'wa Itunda, sima pihe uhege pa msalaba!”
Kumatungo ehali yeyo yeyo ekulu a makuhani aeakumukashifu, palung'wi neaandeki neanyampala, nukulunga,
“Aeuaokoe neangiza, lakini shangauwezilye kiokoa ung'wenso. Nuanso Mutemi wa Ayahudi. Nuasime pihe kupuma mumusalaba, kunso aulungile, unene neng'wa Itunda kuite kumuhuela.
Aeumuhue Itunda. Leki Tunda wamuokoe angeza utakile kunsoko aeulungile, “Unene neng'wana wang'wa Itunda.”
Nawoite enyanyanyi namusulubishilye palung'wi nung'wenso ga atambue makani akumudhihaki.
Imatungo yayo nasaa sita ikatula kiti mihe ehi mpaka esaa tisa.
Naepikile esaa tisa, u Yesu wikalela kusauti nenkulu, “Eloi, Eloi, Lama thabakithani?” wikamaanisha “Itunda ane, Itunda ane, mbona wandeka?”
Ematungo nanso ang'we ao aeimekile pang'wanso aigulye, ekalunga, Ukumitanga Eliya.”
Akamanka ung'wi kuhola sifongo nukizulya ekinywaji nekelulu, ekameeka migulya mumute ekamupa wang'we.
Nao nasagile ekalunga, “Muleki wing'wene, leki kuone kina u Eliya weze muguna.”
U Yesu wikalela hange kwa luli nulukulu wekameheja enkolo akwe.
Goza, Ipazia li itekeelo ailitamukile nkika ibeele kupumila migulya kupikiila pihi. Ni ihi ikakagaka ni matalagwe ikatamuka ipande.
Emakabuli akaluguka nemeele atakatifu edu nualae utulo akioka.
Ekapuma mumakabuli baada aa uiuki wakwe, ekingila mumuji nuutakatifu ekigeeleka edu.
Uakida nuanso nawa naamugozee u Yesu ekaona itetemeko nemakani naakupumela, ekisula uwoa kule nukulunga, “Etai uyu aeng'wana wang'wi Tunda.” Ekagoza kupuma kule.
Aasungu edu amutyatile u Yesu kupuma ku Galilaya ahume kumuhudumela akoeakole pang'wanso ekagozeela kupuma kule.
Mukatekate ao aeukole u Mariamu Magdalena, Mariamu mama akwe Yakobo nu Joseph, nu mama waana ang'wa Zebedayo.
Naepikile mpende awezile muntu mugole kupuma Arimathaya, nae witangwa Yusufu, kuite nuyu nuanso aemumanyisigwa wang'wa Yesu.
Aewendile kung'wa Pilato wekalompa umeele wang'wa Yesu. Kuite u Pilato wekalagelya apegwe.
U Yusufu wekauhola umweele akautunga ung'wenda numuza,
wekaulalesha mikabuli nipya naeulezepilye wekalechonga mumwamba.
U Mariamu Magdalena nu Mariamu numungiza akole hapo aeikie kugozela ikabuli.
Uluhiku nautyatie kina uluhiku nula maandalio, e akulu amakuhani ne Mafarisayo aeilingee palung'wi kung'wa Pilato.
Ekamuela, “Mukulu kukembukile kina imatungo nuanso numudanganyifu naeukele ukole mupanga, aulungile, Baada amahiku atatu ukiioka hange.
Kululo lagilya kina ikabuli lelindwe salama mpaka uluhiku lakatatu. Kuite, eamanyisigwa akwe awezilye kezakumia nukulunga kuantu, “Wioka kupuma mwaashi. Nuudanganyifu wamwisho ukutula ubee kukela naakwanza.
U Pilato wekaaela, “Holi ealinzi. Longoli mitume muhali ausalama pamuwezeye.”
Kuite akalongola nukituma pikabuli kutula usalama ukole, igwe lekagongwa umuhuli nukueka ealinzi.
Baadaye empende uluhiku la Sabato, elyoa naelakapuma kuhumbela luhiku lang'wandyo nulijuma, Mariamu Magdalena, nu Mariamu numungeza azele kulegoza ikabuli.
Goza aelekole itetemeko ikulu, kunsoko umalaeka wang'wa Mukulu ausimile wekalepingilitya igwe, hange wekikaela.
Esula akwe ae ehanganga umeme, neang'wenda akwe ae elu anga etheluji.
Ealinzi neanso ekizula uwoa ekatu anga eashi.
Umalaeka nuanso wekaalengasa easungu neanso wekalunga,'' lekikogopi kondogoelye mine kina mukumuduma Yesu, nausubiwe.
Ukutile apaite, Lakini wioka anga naeumuie. Pembyi muone Ubwana pana aulae.
Longoli halaka muaele emanyisigwa akwe, wiuka kupuma mwashi, goza wamutongeela ku Galilaya. Kung'wanso kukomukumuona. Gozi unene namuela.''
Easungu neanso ekahega pang'wanso pikabuli halaka ekaze akete uwoa ao niloeligwi ikulu, hange ekamanka kuaela eamanyisigwa akwe.
Goza U Yesu wikatankana neenso nukulunga,''Salamu,'' Easunguneanso aeazile ekaamba emegulu akwe, hage ekamukulya.
Ite U Yesu wekaaela,'' lekikogopi, Longoli muaele eanya ndugu akwe atongele Kugalilaya. Kung'wanso akumona.''
Ematungo nanso easungu naalongoe, goza baadhi aalinzekenda kumujini nukuaela aekulu amkuhani emakani ehinaapumie.
Emakuhani naatankanile neanyampala kikoelya emakani nanso palug'wi neenso, Aeapumilye keasi kekulu nekampia kwa alinzi neanso.
Ekaaela,'' Aeli neangiza ite, Eamanyisigwa ang'wa Yesu aeazile utiku ekia umweele wang'wa Yesu imatungo usese azakulae.
Hange etaalifa eye angemupikile uliwali, usese kuumushawishi nukumuhegelya unyenye emashaka ehi.''
Kuite easkali neanso ekaihola impia ninyanso nukituma anga naalagewe. Impola izi ikenela kule kwa ayahundi nayatuile uu mpaka elelo.
Lakini ametume neanso kumi na moja ekalongola ku Galilaya, kumulema nuanso naualagie.
Neenso namuine, ekamukulya, lakini baadhi ao ekakisha.
U Yesu wekeza kung'waao wekaaela wekalunga,'' Mpewe uhumi wehi muunkumbigulu nukilunde.
Kuite longoli muaifanye indugu yehi itule amanyisigwa ane. Abadisi kulina lang'wa Tata. nele nela ng'wana nu ng'wa ung'welu.
Amanyisi kumaamba emakani ehi naenumuie, Goza unenkole palung'wi nunyenye mahiku ehi. mpaka empelo aunkumbigulu.
Uwu ingi ng'wandyo nua nkani ninza niang'wa Yesu Kristo, Ng'wana wang'wa Itunda.
Anga ni ikilisigwe nu munyakidagu uIsaya, “Gozeela, kumulagiilya u mutung'wa nuane ntongeela ako, ung'wi nuikazipiilya i nzila niako.
Luli nula muntu nuitangaa mihaka, “Mikondeelyi i nzila a Mukulu; Igooli i nzila niakwe.”
uYohana ai uzile, wazoja mihaka nu kutanantya wogigwa nua kila itunu ku ulekelwa nua milandu.
Ihi ihi a ku Yudea ni antu ihi nia ku Yerusalemu ai alongoe kitalakwe. Ai atulaa akogigwa nu ng'wenso mu mongo nua Yordani, aze ila itunu ku milandu ao.
uYohana ai watulaa utugae ng'wenda nua mauli a ngamia nu mukoha nua ndili mu kilino nikakwe, hangi ai watulaa ukulya ngaga nu uki nua mihaka.
Ai utanantilye nu kuligitya, “Ukoli ung'wi upembilye ze yakilaa unene munya ngulu ikolo kukila unene, hangi nimugila u unoneli ga nu kutuna pihi nu kutungula i mikoha a ilatu niakwe.
Unene ai numogilye ku mazi, kuiti nuanso ukumoja unyenye ku Ng'wau Ng'welu.”
Ai ipumie mu mahiku nanso kina uYesu ai uzile kupuma ku Nazareti a ku Galilaya, hangi ai wogigwe nu Yohana mu mongo nua Yordani.
Itungo uYesu nai uhumbukile kupuma mu mazi, ai wihengile ilunde ligalanukile ng'walyi nu Ng'wau Ng'welu ukusima pihi migulya akwe anga i nkunda.
Nu luli ai lupumiie milunde, “ Uewe ingi Ng'wana nuane mulowa, Ndoeigwe nangaluu nu ewe.”
Uugwa nkua ing'wi u Ng'wau Ng'welu akamusinja kulongola mihaka.
Ai ukoli mihaka mahiku makumi anne, wazegeng'wa nu Mulugu, Ai watulaa palung'wi ni ikali nia mihaka, nia malaika ai amuaiiye.
Itungili ze yakilaa uYohana kuambwa, uYesu ai uzile ku Galilaya wazetanantya inkani ninza niang'wa Itunda,
wazeligitya, “Itungo lakondaniila, nu utemi nuang'wa Itunda wahumbeela. Ili itunu nu kuhuiila mu nkani ninza.”
Hangi wazekila mu mpelo a luzi nula Galilaya, ai umihengile uSimioni nu Andrea muluna wang'wa Simioni azegumila i nyavu niao mu luzi, kunsoko ai atulaa avua nsamaki.
uYesu ai uatambuie, “Pembyi, ntyati, hangi kumuzipya avua antu.”
Ni nkua ing'wi ai alekile i nyavu hangi akamutyata.
Itungo uYesu naiwagenda kahelu iniino, ai umihengile uYakobo ng'wana wang'wa Zebedayo nu Yohana muluna nuakwe; ai atulaa mi ilinga akuzipya nyavu.
Katungo akaitanga ni enso ai amulekile u tata nuao uZebedayo mukati ilinga ni anyamulimo nia kugulwa, akamutyata.
Nai akapika ku Kapernaumu, luhiku nula kusupya, uYesu ai wingie mi itekeelo nu kumanyisa.
Aka ukuilwa u umanyisa nuakwe. ku iti ai watulaa ukuamanyisa anga muntu naiza ukete uhumi hangi shanga anga amanyi.
Itungo lilo liilo ai ukoli nu muntu mi itekeelo nilao nai ukete nu hing'wi, hangi ai uzogooye,
wazeligitya, “Kukete ntuni nika kituma nu ewe, Yesu nua ku Nazereti? Uzile ku ulimilya? Nukulingile wi nyenyu. U ewe ingi Ng'welu wing'wene nuang'wa Itunda!”
uYesu ai umukenee u hing'wi nu kuligitya, “Kilaga hangi upume mukati akwe!”
Nu hing'wi ai umugwisilye pihi hangi akapuma kitalakwe itungo wazelila ku luli nula migulya.
Ni antu ihi ai akuiwe, iti gwa akikolya kila ung'wi, “iki ingi ntuni? Umanyisa ugeni ukete uhumi? Ga nukulagiilya ia hing'wi nienso aku mukulya!”
Nu lukani kutula ng'wenso nkua ing'wi lukasapatila kila kianza mukati a mukoa wihi nua Galilaya
Hangi nkua ing'wi ze yakilaa kupuma kunzi itekeelo, ai ingi mi ito nilang'wa Simioni nu Andrea aze akoli nu Yakobo nu Yohana.
Itungili mukwingwa nuang'wa Simioni ai watula ulae mulwae, ni nkua ing'wi ai amutambuie uYesu inkani niakwe.
Iti gwa ai uzile, ai umuambile ku mukono, nu kumunyansula migulya; ulwae ukahega kitalakwe, hangi wakandya ku a aiilya.
Mpindi nanso itungo ilyoa lakondya kulimila, ai amuletee kitalakwe ihi nai atulaa alwae, ang'wi nai akete i ahing'wi.
Kisali kihi ai kilingiie palung'wi pa mulango.
Ai uagunile idu nai atulaa alwae a kila ulwae nu kupumya ahing'wi idu, ila shanga ai ulekee hing'wi kuligitya ku nsoko ai amulingile.
Ai u ukile dau maniabwa, itungo nai ikili kiti; ai uhegile nu kulongola nkika a kinkunku nu kulompa kuko.
uSimioni ni ihi nai atulaa palung'wi nu ng'wenso ai amudumile.
Ai amuligilye hangi akamutambuila, “Kila ung'wi uku uduma”
Ai uatambuie, “Kwini kianza kingiiza, kunzi mu isali ni ipilimikiiye, iti nihume kutanantya nuko ga. Yiyo nsoko aza nzile apa.”
Ai ulongoe waze ukiie i Galilaya ihi, waze tanantya mu matekeelo ao nu kuapatya ia hing'wi.
Munya mbili ung'wi ai uzile kitalakwe. Ai watulaa ukumusinja; ai utugamile nu kumutambuila, “Anga ize uloilwe, uhumile kunzipya ntule ni muza.”
Waze usuntilwe ni kinya uwai, uYesu ai ugooe u mukono nuakwe nu kumuamba, akamuila, “Ndoilwe, Utule u muza.”
Itungo ling'wi i mbili ikamupuma, hangi ai uzipigwe kutula muza.
uYesu akamukania itaki nu kumuila walongole itungo ling'wi.
Ai umutambuie, “Kendegeela shanga uligitilye lukani ku wihi, kuiti longola, wiambye kung'wa kuhani, hangi upumye isongelyo ku nsoko a weligwa naiza uMusa ai ulagiiye, anga ukuiili kitalao.”
Kuiti ai ulongoe nu kandya kumutambula kila ung'wi nu kenelya u lukani ikilo ga nu Yesu shanga ai uhumile hangi kingila mu kisali ku ulyuuku. Iti gwa ai wikiie kianza nika kinkunku ni antu ai azile kitalakwe kupuma kila nkika.
Nai usukile ku Kapernaumu ze yakilaa mahiku masheenyu, ai ikumukile kina ai ukoli mi ito.
Antu idu nangaluu ai atulaa ilundiie pang'wanso hangi shanga ai limoli i lyoma hangi, ga nilo nila pa mulango, nu Yesu ai uligitilye lukan kitalao.
Uugwa ang'wi a antu ai azile kitalakwe nai amuletile muntu nai watulaa ukule igandi; antu anne ai atulaa amukenkile.
Itungo nai alemilwe kumuhumbeela kunsoko a iubi nila antu, ai agumue migulya a kianza pang'wanso nai ukoli. Hangi nai atula akondyaa kutobola ibolomyo, ai asimilye u ulili naiza u muntu nai ukule igandi ai watulaa ulae.
Nai wihengile u uhuiili nuao, uYesu ai umutambuie u muntu nai ukule igandi, “ng'waane, i milandu ako alekelwa.”
Kuiti ang'wi ao a amanyi awo nai akoli ikie pang'wanso ai ikoiye mu nkolo niao.
“Uhumile uli u muntu uyu kuligiya iti? Uku kuna! Nyenyu nuihuma kulekela i milandu kwaala Itunda wing'wene duu?”
Itngo uYesu nai ulingile mu nkolo akwe nai atulaa akusiga mukati ao akola. Ai ua tambuie, “Ku niki mukusiga iti mu nkolo nianyu?
Ni liuli ni ipepeele ikilo kuligitya ku muntu nu kule igandi, 'Milandu ako alekelwaa' ang'wi kuligitya 'imike, hola u ulili nuako, hangi uende?'
Kuiti iti alije kulinga kutula u Ng'wana nuang'wa Adamu ukete u humi nua kulekela i milandu mi ihi, ai umutambuie uyo nai ukule igandi.
“Nukutambuie u ewe, nyansuka, hola u mukeka nuako, hangi ulongole kito nilako.”
Ai wimikile hangi nkua ing'wi akahola u mukeka nuakwe, hangi ai ulongoe kunzi a numba ntongeela a kila muntu, iti ihi ai akuiwe hangi akaminkiilya Itunda ikulyo, hangi akaligitya “Nangaluu, kukili kaya kihenga ikani anga ili.”
Ai ulongoe hangi mpelo a luzi, ni iumbi lihi nila antu ai azile kitalakwe, hangi waka amanyisa.
Nai watula ukukila ai umihengile uLawi ng'wana wang'wa Alfayo wikie mu nkika a kuhanguilya i kodi hangi akamuila, “Ntyate.” Ai wimikile nu kumutyata.
Hangi itungo uYesu nai watulaa ukulya indya mu nyumba ang'wa Lawi, ahangulya kodi idu ni antu niakete i milandu ai atulaa akulya nu Yesu ni amanyisigwa akwe, ku nsoko ai atulaa idu ni enso ai amutyatile.
Itungo i amanyi, naza atulaa Afarisayo, nai akihenga kina uYesu ukulya ni antu anya milandu ni ahangulya kodi, ai a atambuie i amanyisigwa akwe, “Ku niki ukulya ni ahangulya kodi ni anya milandu?”
Itungo uYesu nai wakija iti ai uatambuie, “Antu niakete u upanga mu muili shanga amutakile u mukiliki; Ingi antu nia lwae ing'wene wawo amutakile. Shanga ai nzile kuitanga i antu niakete itai ane, kuiti antu ni akete i milandu.”
Amanyisigwa ang'wa Yohana ni Afarisayo ai atulaa akudilya kulya. Hangi ang'wi a antu ai azile kitalakwe nu kumuila, “Ku niki i aanyisigwa ang'wa Yohana ni Afarisayo idila kulya, kuiti i amanyisigwa ako shanga akudila kulya?
uYesu ai uatambuie, “Itii niamoli mu winga ahumile kudila kulya itungo u mukulu nua winga waze utuile ukoli palung'wi ni enso? ku lihi u mukulu nua winga anga watule ukoli palung'wi ni enso shanga ahumile kudila kulya.”
Kuiti mahiku apembilye itungo u mukulu nua winga nuika hegigwa kitalao, nu mu mahiku nanso ni enso akudilya kulya.
Kutili u muntu nuihilita i kilaka ni kigeni nika ng'wenda mu ng'wenda nui taho, anga itule i kilaka kikutaluka kupuma mu nilanso, ni kigeni kitaluka kupuma mi itaho, hangi ikutula nu utamukwaa ubibi.
Kutili muntu wihi nuikitila i magai ni maza mu ntunda ni nkakilu, anga itule iti imagai akubadula i ntunda hangi yahi ibiili magai ni itunda ikulimila. Badala akwe, ika imagai ni maziza mu ntunda ni nziza.
Mu luhiku nula kusupya uYesu ai ukiile mu migunda ing'wi, ni amanyisigwa akwe akandya kuhola imatita ang'wi a ngano.
Ni Afarisayo akamuila, “Goza, ku niki akituma i kintu naiza ingi nsuta ni ilagiilyo mu luhiku nula kusupya?”
Ai uatambuie, “Shanga ai musomile iko nai witumile uDaudi nai watula mu u ula nua nzala—Ng'wenso palung'wi ni antu nai akoli palung'wi nu ng'wenso?
Iti nai ulongoe mu ito nilang'wa Itunda itungo nilang'wa Abiathari nai watulaa kuhani nu mukulu nu kulya u mukate nai uikilwe ntongeela—naza ituile nsuta a malagiilyo ku muntu wihi kulya kwaala akuhani— hangi ai uinkiiye ga ni ang'wi a awo nai atulaa palung'wi nu ng'wenso
uYesu ai uligitilye, U luhiku nula kusupya ai litumilwe ku nsoko a ana adamu, shanga ng'wana adamu ku nsoko a luhiku nula kusupya.
Ku lulo, u Ng'wana nuang'wa Adamu ingi mukulu, ga kuluhiku nula kusupya.
Ni hangi ai wingie mukati itekeelo nu mung'wanso ai umoli muntu ukete mukono ukule igandi.
Ang'wi a antu ai atulaa akumutyatiila ku ukupi kihenga kina anga ize ukuguna luhiku nula kusupya iti kina amusemele.
uYesu ai umutambuie u muntu nu kete u mukono ukule igandi. “Humbuka wimike pakati i umbi ili.”
Uugwa aka atambuila i antu. “Itii ingi taine kituma mulimo nu uza luhiku nula kusupya ang'wi kituma ni shanga tai ane; Kunguna likalo ang'wi kubulaga?” Kuiti akasaga ihi twi.
Aka agozeela ku ikuo, waze uhukilye ku nsoko a ukaku nua nkolo niao, hangi akamutambuila u muntu uyo, “Goola u mukono nuako.” akaugoola nu Yesu akamuguna u mkono nuakwe.
Afarisayo akalongola kunzi hangi itungo akazipya isui palung'wi ni Aherode ku ng'waakwe iti kumubulaga.
Uugwa uYesu, palung'wi ni amanyisigwa akwe, ai alongoe mu luzi, ni i umbi ikulu nila antu ai limutyatile ize lipembeeye ku Galilaya nu ku Uyahudi
nu kupuma ku Yerusalemu nu kupuma ku Idumaya ntongeela a Yorodani ni kisali nika Tiro ni Sidoni, i umbi ikulu, nai likija kila i kintu nai watulaa ukituma, akapembya kitalakwe.
Hangi ai uatambuie i amanyisigwa akwe kuzipiilya u mulinga nu uniino ku nsoko akwe ku nsoko a iumbi, iti kina aleke kumutunyiilya.
Ku nsoko ai ugunile idu, iti kila u muntu nai watulaa nu lwago ai watulaa ni nsula a kumupikiila iti wamuambe.
Pihi i ahing'wi nai amuine, ai agwie pihi ntongeela akwe nu kulila, nu kuligitya, “U ewe ingi wi Ng'wana wang'wa Itunda.”
Ai ualagiiye ku kukomangiila aleke kituma wakumuke.
Ai ulongoe migulya a lugulu, nu kuitanga nai ualoilwe, hangi akalongola kitalakwe.
Aka aholania ikumi na abiili (nai uitangile itumi), iti kina atule palung'wi nu ng'wenso hangi wahume kualagiilya kutanantya,
nu kutula nu uhumi nua kupumya i ahing'wi.
Hangi aka aholania ikumi na abiili; Simioni nai uminkiiye ilina nila Petro,
Yakobo ng'wana wang'wa Zebedayo, nu Yohana muluna nuakwe u Yakobo, nai winkiigwe i lina nila Bonagesi, awo ingi, ana nia mulilo,
nu Andrea, Filipo, Bartholomayo, Mathayo, Tomaso, Yakobo ng'wana wang'wa Alfayo, Thadayo, Simioni Mukananayo,
nu Yuda Iskariote, naiza uku mugumaniilya.
Uugwa ai ulongoe ki ito, ni umbi nila antu akapembya palung'wi hangi, aleng'we ga nu kulya ga nu mukate.
Familia akwe nai akija u lukani nulanso, akalongola kumuamba, kuiti akaligitya, “Waputwa ni mahala.”
Amanyi nai azile kupuma ku Yerusalemu ai aligitilye, “Uhalinkaniwe nu Beelzebuli,” nu “Ku mukulu nua a hing'wi ukupumya i a hing'wi.”
uYesu ai uitangile kitalakwe nu kuligitya ni enso ku mpyani, “Kinya uli uMulugu wahume kumupumya uMulugu?
Anga ize utemi ukugalanuka ukola, utemi nuanso shanga uhumile kimika.
Anga ize ito likugalanuka ikola, ito nilanso shanga lihumile kimika.
Anga ize uMulugu ukunyansuka nsuta akwe mukola nu kugalanuka, hangi ukutula wapika mpelo akwe.
Kuiti kutili ga nung'wi nuhumile kingila mukati ito nila muntu ni munya ngulu nu kia i intu niakwe bila kumutunga u munyangulu hanza, hangi uugwa kilingiila ni kimoli mi ito.
Tai kumutambuila, milandu ihi nia ana a antu ikulekelwa, palung'wi nu ukuni naza akutambula,
kuiti wihi nuika mukuna u Ng'wau Ng'welu shanga ukulekelwa lukulu, ila ukete ugazi nua mulandu nua kali na kali.”
uYesu ai ulitambue ili ku nsoko ai atulaa akuligitya, “Ukete hing'wi.”
Uugwa u nyinya nuakwe ni aluna akwe ai apembilye nu kimika kunzi. Akamulagiilya muntu, kumitanga.
Ni iumbi nila antu nai latulaa likie pakupi nu ng'wenso akamutambuila, “u ia ako ni aluna ako akoli kunzi, hangi akuuduma u ewe.”
Ai uasukiiye, “Ingi nyenyu u ia ane ni aluna ane?”
Ai uagozee nai atulaa ikie amupilimikiiye, nu kuligitya, “Goza, awa ingi a ia ane ni aluna ane!
Wihi nuitumaa u ulowa nuang'wa Itunda, muntu nuanso ingi muluna ane, hangi ng'waitu, hangi ia ane.”
Hangi ai wandilye kumanyisa mu mpelompelo a luzi. Ni iumbi ikulu likilundiila likamupilimikiilya, akingila mukati i ilinga mu luzi, nu kikie. Iumbi lihi nai likoli mu mpelo a luzi mu nshemba.
Hangi aka amanyisa makani idu ku mpyani, hangi akaligitya kitalao ku umanyisa nuakwe.
Tegeelyi, mutemeli ai ulongoe kutemela.
Nai wakatula ukutemela, ing'wi nia mbeu ai igwie mu nzila, ni nyunyi ikapembya ikailya.
Mbeu i nzuya ai igwie mu matalagwe, naiza kutili ni mahalu idu. Itungo ikanyala, ku nsoko ai ngila anga mahalu nakondaniie.
Kuiti i lyoa nai litolokile, ai inyaile, ku nsoko ai ngila anga mili, ikuma.
Mbeu inzuya ai igwie pakati a mija. iMija ikakula nu kuitunyiilya, hangi shanga ikapa inkali yihi.
Mbeu i nzuya ai igwie mu mahalu ni maza hangi ai ipee i nkali itungo nai yukukula nu kungeeleka, inzuya ai ipee nkua makumi ataatu ikilo, ni nzuya makumi mutandaatu, ni nzuya igana.”
Hangi wakaligitya, “Wihi nukete i akutwi ni akija, nu ije!”
uYesu nai wakatula wing'wene, awo nai akoli pakupi nu ng'wenso nawo ni ikumi na abiili ai amukoiye kutula i mpyani.
Akaligitya kitalao, “Kitalanyu minkiigwe kinkunku nika utemi nuang'wa Itunda. Kuiti ku niakoli kunzi kila i kintu ingi mpyani,
iti anga agoze, uu igoza, kuiti shanga ihenga, hangi ku lulo niakija uu ijaa, kuiti shanga ilinga, anga ize shanga uu aza azee mupiluka Itunda ai uzee alekela.”
Hangi akaligiya kitalao, “Itii shanga mulingile i mpyani iyi? Mukuhuma uli kulinga i mpyani ni ingiiza?
Mutemeli ai utemee lukani.
Ing'wi ingi awo nai agwie mu mpelo a anzila, kianza u lukani naza lutemewe. Hangi nai igulye, itungo u Mulugu akapembya nu kuluhola u lukani naiza lutemewe mukati ao.
Hani ang'wi ao ingi awo nai atemewe migulya amatalagwe, naza, nai igulye u lukani, ku ukau akulusingiilya ku ulowa.
Hnagi agila imili ihi mukati ao, kuiti igimya ku itungo ikupi. Halafu lwago nu wagigwa ni ipembilye ku nsoko a lukani, itungo ikumpyaa.
Hangi ang'wi ingi awo nai atemewe mu mija. Akulija u lukani.
Kuiti unyong'wa nu ihi. ukongelwa nua nsao, ni nsula a makani mangiiza, wi ingiila nu kulutunyiilya u lukani, nu kuleng'wa kupaa inkali.
Uugwa akoli awo naza atemewe mu mahalu ni maza. Akulija u lukani nu kulusingiilya nu kupa i nkali; ang'wi makumi ataatu, hangi ang'wi makumi mutandatu, hangi ang'wi igana ling'wi.”
uYesu aka atambuila, “Itii iiza wileta u lumuli mukati ito nu kuluika pihi a nkapu, ang'wi pihi a ulili? Wiluletaa mukati nu kuluika migulya a ishupaka.
Ku nsoko kutili kihi nikipihile naiza shanga kiku kumuka, hangi kutili i kinkunku naiza shanga kikuikwa kihenga.
Anga ize ukoli nukete i akutwi a kija, nu ije!”
Aka atambuila, “Tuli miakendegeeli ku iko ni mukukija, ku nsoko u ugemeelya ni mukugemeelya, kiko ni mukagemeeligwa, hangi kikongeligwa kitalanyu.
Ku nsoko nuanso nukete, ukinkiiligwa ikilo, hangi uyo nimugila, kupuma kitalakwe ikuholwa ga nizo nuikete.”
Hangi akaligitya, “Utemi nuang'wa Itunda wimpyanigwe nu muntu nai utemee i mbeu mu mahalu.
Nai wakalala u utiku nu kuuka i kidaudau, ni mbeu ikaheluka nu kukula, Ga ni uu shanga ulingile nai ipumie.
Ihi ipumyaa i mbeu nkola; hanza matutu, alafu ulua, alafu mbeu niakagupaa.
Hangi itungo imbeu ni ikatula ailyaa itungo witwalaa uzolo, ku nsoko i maogola apikiila.”
Hangi akaligitya, “kuimpyanie u utemi nuang'wa itunda ni kintu kii, ang'wi kutumile mpyani kii ku uganula?
Ingi anga i mbeu a haradali, naiza ai itemewe ingi niino nangaluu kukila i mbeu yihi mihi.
Ga, ni itungo naza itemewe, ikukula nu kutula nkulu ikilo nila mimea ihi mu shuli, hangi izipyaa ntaambi nkulu, ga ni nyunyi nia kilunde ihumaa kuzipya iuyi niao mu mululi nuakwe.”
Ku mpyani idu ai umanyisilye hangi ai uligitilye u lukani kitalao, ku upikiilo nai uhumile kulinga,
hangi shanga ai uligitilye ni enso bila mpyani. Kuiti itungo nai wakatula wing'wene duu, aka aganuila kila i kintu i amanyisigwa akwe.
Mu luhiku nulanso, itungo nila mpindi nai lipikiie, akaligitya kitalao, “Kweni i nkika a kabiili.”
Iti gwa akalileka i umbi, akamuhola uYesu, itungo nilanso yakondaa ai watula mukati ilinga. Malinga mauya ai atulaa palung'wi nu ng'wenso.
Nu ng'wega utaki nua kimpupu ni maingu ai atulaa akingila mukati a mulinga nu mulinga ai wakondyaa kutula wizula.
Kuiti uYesu mukola ai ukoli mu shetri, ulae mu muto. Akamutambuila, azeligitya, “Ng'walimu, shanga ulingile kina usese kuusha?”
Hangi akauka, akaukenela u ng'wega nu kuluila u luzi, “Itule ihi twii, ulyuuku.” Ung'wega ukapela, hangi ai ituile nu ulyuuku ukulu.
Hangi akaligitya kitalao, “Ku niki mukitumba? Itii mukili miagila u uhuiili?”
Akizuilwa nu woa ukulu mukati ao hangi akitambulya enso ku enso, “Uyu ingi nyenyu hangi, ku nsoko ga nu ng'wega nu luzi ikumugombya.”
Nai akapembya kupikiila nkika ingiiza a luzi, mu mukoa nua Gerasi.
Hangi kupumpugila itungo uYesu naiwatulaa ukupuma kunzi ilinga, muntu nukete u hing'wi ai uzile kitalakwe kupuma mu ibiila.
Muntu uyu ai wikiie mu ibiila. Kutili nai uhumile kumugilya ikilo, kutili ga nu ku minyororo.
Ai watulaa utungilwe matungo iduu ku mpingu ni minyororo. Kutili ga nu ng'wi nai ukete i ngulu nia kumukilya.
Utiku nu mung'wi waze ukoli mu ibiila nu mu malugulu, ai wilila nu kitemanga u ng'wenso mukola ku magwe ni migi.
Nai wakamihenga uYesu ku kaheelu, akamankiila kung'wakwe nu kutuna ntongeela akwe.
Ai uleile ku luli lukulu, “Uloilwe nukutendele ntuni, Yesu ng'wana wang'wa Itunda nukoli migulya nangaluu? Ku usinja kung'wa Itunda mukola, leka kunaja.
Ku nsoko ai watulaa wamuila, “Mupume u muntu uyu, u ewe hing'wi.”
Nu ng'wenso ai umukoiye, “Lina nilako ingi nyenyu?” Nuanso akamusuliilya, “Lina nilane ingi Legion, ku nsoko kukoli kidu.”
Ai umusingilye hangi ni hangi waleke kuatwala kunzi a mukoa.
Itungili idale ikulu nila ngulima ai likoli likuding'wa migulya a lugulu,
ni enso ai amusingilye, azeligitya, “Kulagiilye ku ngulima; kingile mu kati yao.”
Iti gwa ai uagombilye; ia hing'wi ai amupumile nu kingila mukati a ngulima, ni nyenso ai imankile pihi a lugulu kupikiila mu luzi, hangi kupikiila ngulima magana a nzogu a biili ikalimilila mu luzi.
Hangi awo nai atulaa akudima i ngulima ai amankile nu kupumya u lukani nula iko nai kipumie mu kisali nu mi ihi. Uugwa antu idu ai apumile kulongola kihenga nai kipumie.
Uugwa ai apembilye kung'wa Yesu hangi ai amihengile u muntu nai wahalinkaniwe nu hing'wi nai ukete idale —wikie pihi, utugawe, hangi aze ukoli mu mahala akwe akondaniie, ni enso ai itumbile.
Awo nai atulaa ihengile nai kipumie ku muntu nai watulaa uhalinkaniwe nu hing'wi ai a atambuie nai kipumie kitalakwe ga ni kutula i ngulima.
Ni enso akandya kumusinja wahege mu mukoa nuao.
Hangi nai wakatula ukingila mukati i linga, muntu nai watulaa uhalinkaniwe nia hing'wi ai umusingilye kina alongole palung'wi nu ng'wenso.
Kuiti shanga ai umugombilye, kuiti ai umutambuie, “Longola ki ito nilako nu ku antu niako, hangi uatambuile aza ukutendee Mukulu, nu ukende naza ukinkiiye.”
Uugwa ai ulongoe nu kandya kutanantya i makani makulu naiza uYesu witumile kitalakwe mu Dekapoli, ni kila ung'wi ai ukuiwe.
Hangi itungo nai wakaputa hangi nkika i ngiiza, mukati ilinga, iumbi ikulu likilingiila kumupilimikiilya, nai ukoli mpelo a luzi.
Hangi ung'wi nu a lukolongo ni i tekeelo, nai witangwaa Yairo, ai uzile, hangi nai umuhengile, ai ugwie mu migulu akwe.
Akamusija ikilo ni ikilo, wazeligitya, “Munaanso nu ane nu muniino wahumbeela kusha. Ku usinja, pembya nu kuika i mikono ako migulya akwe iti kina wahume kulija upanga nu kikie.”
Iti gwa ai ulongoe palung'wi nu ng'wenso. ni i umbi ikulu ai limutyatile ni enso ai akumunyempa pakupi aze amupilimikiiye.
Ai ukoli nu musungu naiza i sakami akwe ai atulaa ipumaa ku myaka ikumi na ibiili.
Ai wagilee nia kukonda pihi a akiliki idu hangi ai watumie kila i kintu nai watuile ni kenso. Ga ni iti shanga akagunika ku kintu kihi. kuiti badala akwe akakilinkiila kutula ni hali mbibi.
Ai wigulye i nkani kutula uYesu. Iti gwa ai upembilye ku nyuma akwe itungo nai watulaa ukugenda mukati i umbi, nu ng'wenso ai utenilye u ng'wenda nuakwe.
Ku nsoko ai uligitilye, “Anga niatenie i ang'wenda ni akwe udu, nikatula ni mupanga.”
Nai utenilye, kupung'wa i sakami ikapela, hangi ai wigulye mu muili nuakwe kina ai wagunwaa kupuma mu lwago nulakwe
Hangi kupumpugiilya uYesu akalinga mukati akwe mukola kina ngulu imupumile. Hangi ai upilukile kunu nu kunu mi iumbi nila antu nu kukolya, “Ingi nyenyu nutenilye u ng'wenda nuane?”
Amanyisigwa akwe ai amutambuie, “Ukihenga i umbii ili likutunyiiye likupilimikiiye, nu ewe ukuligitya, 'Ingi nyenyu nu ntenilye?'”
Kuiti uYesu ai ugozile kunu nu kunu kihenga naiza watulaa witumile ili.
Musungu, waze ulingile nai kipumie kitalakwe, ai witumbile nu kukagata. Ai upembilye hangi ai ugwie pihi ntongeela akwe nu kumuila i tai ihi.
Ai uligitilye kitalakwe, “Munanso, uhuiili nuako wakuzipya utule u mupanga. Longola ku ulyuuku hangi ugunwe kupuma mu ulwae nuako.”
Nai watulaa ukuligitya, ang'wi a antu ai apembilye kupuma kung'a lukolongo nua itekeelo, azeligitya, “U munanso nuako wakuza. Ku niki kulongoleka kumunyoma u ng'walimu?”
Kuiti uYesu nai wakija naza akukiligiya, ai umutambuie u lukolongo nu itekeelo, Leka kitumba. Huiila udu.”
Shanga ai umugombilye wihi kitongelya nu ng'wenso kwaala uPetro, Yakobo, nu Yohana muluna nuakwe uYakobo.
Ai apembilye mi ito nilang'wa lukolongo nui itekeelo nu ng'wenso ai wihengile unyong'wa, kulila kidu nu kuhongeelya.
Nai wakingila mi ito, ai uatambuie, “ Ku niki mukusiga ikulu hangi ku niki mukulila? uMung'yinya akili kusha ila ulae.”
Ai amuhekile, kuiti nuanso, ai uapumilye ihi kunzi, ai umuhoile utata nua ng'wana nu nyinya ni awo nai atulaa palung'wi nu ng'wenso, hangi ai wingie mukati nai umoli u ng'wana.
Ai u uhoile u mukono nua ng'wana hangi ai umutambuie, “Talitha koum,” naiza ingi kuligitya, “Munanso muniino, ku utambuila, uka.”
Kupumpugiilya u ng'wana ai u ukile nu kugenda. (ku nsoko ai watulaa ni ilika nila myaka ikumi na ibiili). Hangi kupumpugiilya ai a ambilwe nu ukuilwa ukulu.
Ai ulagiiye ku ngulu kina kutili wihi utakiwe kulinga kutula ili. Hangi ai uatambuie aminkiilye u munanso nuanso indya.
Hangi akahega pang'wanso nu kulongola mu kisali kao, ni amanyisiga akwe akamutyata.
Luhiku nula kusupya nai likapika. ai wandilye kumanyisa mu Itekeelo. Antu idu ai amigulye hangi akakuilwa. Akaligitya, Uligilye pii u umanyisa uwu?” Ingi upolo kii uwu nuinkiigwe?” Ukituma uli u ukuilwa uwu ku mikono akwe?”
“Itii uyu shanga yuyo u mulanda mabada, ng'wana wang'wa Mariamu hangi muluna nuao ia Yakobo, Yose, Yuda nu Simioni? Itii i aluna akwe nia kisugu shanga ikie papa paapa palung'wi nu sese?” Hangi shanga ikaloeligwa nu Yesu.
uYesu aka atambuila, “U munyakidagu shanga wiulyaa ikulyo, kwaala mu kisali nikakwe ni mukati a aluna akwe nia mi ito nilakwe.”
Shanga ai uhumile kituma u ukuilwa pang'wanso, iti ai uaikiiye mikono alwae asheenyu aka aguna.
