Ng'wau Ng'welu, mazi ni sakami. Awa ni ataatu igombyaa. (Komaniilya; Imakani aya, “Tata, Lukani, nu Ng'wau Ng'welu” shanga igeelekile mu mbugulu ni nziza nia kale.)
Anga ize kiusingiilya u ukuiili nua ana adamu, u ukuiili nuang'wa Itunda ingi ukulu kukila nuanso. Kunsoko u ukuiili nuang'wa Itunda ingi uwu- kina ukete u ukuiili nui kigendi nu Ng'wana nuakwe.
uNg'wenso nu muhuiie uNg'wana nuang'wa Itunda ukete u ukuiili mukati akwe mukola. Hangi wihi ni shanga umuhuiie Itunda umuzipilye kutula muteele, ku nsoko shanga uhuiie u ukuiili naza Itunda u uletile kutula Ng'wana nuakwe.
Nu ukuiili ingi wuwu - kina Itunda ai ukinkiiye upanga nua kali na kali, nu upanga uwu umoli mukati a Ng'wana nuakwe.
Numukete u ng'wana ukete u upanga. Nu mugila ung'wana nuang'wa Itunda mugila u upanga.
Nu mukilisiiye aya muhume kulinga kina mukete upanga nua kali na kali - nu nyenye ni muhuiie mu lina ni la Ng'wana nuang'wa Itunda.
Hangi uwu wuwo ugimya ni ku ukete ntongeela akwe, kina anga kulompe kintu kihi kuniganiila nu ulowa nuakwe, wikijaa.
Hangi anga ize kulingile kina wikijaa - kihi ni kimulompaa kulingile kina kukete iko ni kumulompile.
Anga u muntu nuimihengaa u muluna nuakwe ukituma u mulandu ni shanga witwalinkiilya insha, imutakiwe kulompa nu Itunda ukumi nkiilya u upanga. Kuligitya ku awo naza umulandu nuao ingi uwo nishanga wiletekeelya insha - ukoli u mulandu nui twali nkiilya insha - shanga kuligitya kina utakiwe kulompa kunsoko a mulandu nuanso.
Upiluki wihi ingi mulandu - kuiti ukoli u mulandu ni shanga witwalinkiilya insha.
Kulingile kina nutugilwe nu Itunda shanga witumaa i milandu. Ila nutugilwe nu Itunda wi ikwaa nung'wesno iziza ikali, nu uyo u mubii shanga uhumile kumulemaalya.
Kulingile kina usese ki ang'wa Itunda hangi kulingile kina u unkumbigulu wihi ukoli pihi a utemi nua uyo u mubii.
Ku iti kulingile kina uNg'wana nuang'wa Itunda ai uzile hangi wakinkiiye u ulingi, kina kumulingile nuanso nua tai ni kina kumoli mukati akwe nuanso nua tai, ga nu mu Ng'wana nuakwe uYesu Kristo. Ingi Itunda nua tai nu upanga nua kali na kali.
Ang'yinya alowa, ihuji ni a dudu.
Kupuma ku munyampala kulongela ku musungu ni muholwa ni ana akwe, naza nialoilwe mu tai ni shanga unene duu, ila ni ihi awo nia milingile itai,
kunsoko a tai ni moli mukati itu hangi ni ikikie palung'wi nu sese i kali na kali.
Ukende, upolo, ulyuuku ikutula nu sese kupuma kung'wa Itunda Tata nu kupuma kung'wa Yesu Kilisto, ng'wana nua Tata katikatai nu ulowa.
Ndoilwe nangaluu kina nai ningile ang'wi a ana alongoe mu tai, anga uu udu nai kusingiiye ilagiilyo kupuma kung'wa Tata.
Ni itungili kuusinja uewe, musungu, shanga kina kuuandikila ilagiilyo igeni, ila lilo iti ila nai kukoli ni lyenso pumiila ung'wandyo, kina kutakiwe kilowa usese ku sese. nu uwu wuwo ulowa, kutakiwe kulongoleka, kuniganiila ni ilagiilyo ni lakwe.
Ili lilo ilagiilyo, anga naimigulye pumiila u ng'wandyo, kina mutakiwe kulongoleka mu lilo.
Kunsoko ia kongili idu asapatie mu unkumbigulu, hangi shanga ikulya kina uYesu kilisto ai uzile mu muili, Uyu yuyo mukongili hangi mugilya kilisto.
Ikendegeeli akola kina shanga milimilya imakani ayo naika kondya kitumila mulimo, kuiti iti kina muhume kusingiilya kipegwa ni kikondile.
Wihi nui longolekaa ntoneela nu kikie mu umanyisigwa nuang'wa kilisto, mugila Itunda. Nuanso nuikiie mu umanyisigwa ukete uTata nu Ng'wana ga.
Anga umuntu upembilye kitalanyu hangi shanga wiletaa imanyisigwa ili, Leki kumusingiilyi mi ito ni lanyu hangi leki kumulamushi.
Kunsoko nuimulamushaa wihanguilaa mu ntendo niakwe ni mbibe.
Nkete makani idu ni a kumukilisilya, hangi shanga ndoilwe kumakilisa mitutu nu ung'ole. Kuiti nsigiie kupembya kitalanyu nu kutambula usu ku usu, kina iloeelya ni litu lihume kuzipigwa likondile.
Ana a muluna nu anyu musagulwa akumulamusha.
Munyampala, u-Gayo Mulowa, ninumuloilwe mutai.
Mulowa, kuulompeela ulije ihi ni maza nukutula nu-upanga nu-uza, anga iikolo ako nilijaa.
Ku-itigwa ainumbiiye itai matungo naimbiiwe niiane naiazile pumia wihengi mutai ako, anga uu nukugenda mutai.
Nimugila ilumbi nikulu kukila ili, kija iianaane akugenda mutai.
Mulunaane ukoli mu-uhuili kuapa iiane niaziila,
niiapumilye uwihengi wa ulowaako ntongeela itekeelo, ukunonia iza kuatindikiilya mumihizo-ao kunsokonanso imuloile Itunda.
Ku-itegwa, kunsoko alina, ikalongola sha-ikahola kintu kihi kupuma kuanya-kilungu.
Ku-itegwa, kuasingiilya iantu anga awa, sunga kutule keituma milimo nienso kunsoko atai.
Ai niliandikie iumbi inkani, kunsoko u-Diotrofe uloilwe kutula wang'wandyo muauya, kunu wikutile palung'wi nusese.
Ku-itegwa anganize niisiganiilye intendo yakwe nukuitenda, nukuiligitya inkani nimbe singanguse, sha wigombilye ninkani izi, ung'wenso sha wiasingiilya iauya, sunga ukuagilya niangiiza niakete insula kusingiilya i auyaao nukuazunsa ahege piumbe.
Mulowa, leka kimpyania ni kibii, ingigwa impanie nikiza, uyu nuitumaa nimaza wang'wi- Itunda.
Demotrio, wihengilwe ni-ihi nitai inyenso, nu-sese palung'wi ki-ihengi, uine uwihengi witu watai.
Nkite makani idu nakuuandikila, kuitegwa, siindoilwe kuuandikila kunzila akalamu nu wino.
Nsigile kuuona matungo makupi kuligitye.
Upolo utule palung'wi nuewe. Ahumbaiako akulamukilye, alamushe iahumbaeitu kila muntu ung'wiao kulina lakwe.
Yuda, mutuung'wa wang'wa Yesu kilisto, nu muluna nuakwe uYakobo, ku awo naza itangilwe, ni alowa mung'wa Itunda Tata, ni nai aikilwe ang'wa Yesu kilisto;
ukede nu ulyuuku nu ulowa yongeeligwe kitalanyu.
Alowa, itungo naza ntulaa kituma ukamatiku kumukulisilya unyenye kutula ugunwa witu kihi, ai insingilye kumukilisilya ku nsoko kumusija iti kikilya ku uhuiili u uhuuili niiza aiwatulaa winkiigwenkua ing'wi duu ku ahuiili.
Kunsoko antu a kituunga i ingiiye ku kimpinyi mpinyi mukati anyu - antu naza aikiwe logo kunsok a ulamulwa - antu ni shanga eligwa naza ikailaa u ukende nu ang'wa Itunda witu kuu wii, nu kumuhita uMukulu witu wing'wene nu Mukulu uYesu kilisto.
Itungili ndoilwe kumukimbukiilya unyenye anga ize likoli itungo ai mulingile ku ukondaniili kina uMukulu ai uagunile i antu kupuma ku Misri, kuiti panyambele kualimilya awo nai shanga amuhuiie.
Nu malaika naza shanga asungilye u ukulu nuao akola kuiti akaleka u likalo nu lao Itunda waaikile mu minyololo a kali na kali, mukati a kiti, kunsoko a ulamulwa nua luhiku ulo nu lukulu.
Anga iti iSodoma ni Gomora ni isali ni yiipilimikiiye, naiza yiingiye inkola mu usambo nu kutyata nsula ni shanga nia upuumo. Ai alagiiwe anga mpyani a awo naza agisha mu ulamulwa nua moto nua kali na kali.
Ga ni iti, ku nzila yiyo yiiyo alota ndoti awa ishapulaa ga ni miili ao, nu kuhita u unyangulu, hangi ni ituntaa u uteele kung'wa mukuligwa.
Kuiti ga nu Mikaeli malaika nu mukulu, itungo nai watulaa ukikilya nu mulugu nu kikolenkeelya nu ng'wenso kunsoko a muili nuang'wa Musa, kuiti badala akwe ai uligitilye,
“Mukulu wakupatye” Kuiti antu awa iletaa uteele ku kinya kihi nishanga akilingile. Ni iko nishanga akilingile - iko naiza i ikali ni igila imahala ilingaa ku kupepwa aya yayo ai aagazangilye.
Ukia nu ao ku nsoko agendile mu nzila ang'wa Kaini, nu kuutyata uutumuli nuang'wa Balaamu. Alimiilie mu upiluki nuang'wa Kora.
Awa inge matalagwe mu ilooelya nuanyu nu a ulowa, akilooelya tili ni minyala, akilisa udu ienso. Ingi malunde ni magila imazi, nikenkwaa nu ng'wega, ingi makota nalagae ni magila inkali ni ikule nkua akabiili, ni ipilwe i mili.
Ingi maingu a luzi akete iyogo azepumya i minyala ao akola, Ingi nzota ni yikupilimikiilya niiza u wilwaalu nua kiti uikilwe kunsoko ao ikali na kali
Enoko, nua mupungati mu ulelwa nuan'wa Adamu, ai ulotile kutula enso, wazeligitya “Goza; uMukulu upembilye ni magana ku magana a eligwa niakwe,
iti witume ulamulwa migulya a kila muntu, nu kingilya utumuli ni shanga imukulya Itunda migulya a ntendo ni ao yihi nai akondyaa kituma mu nzila ni shanga ya weligwaa, nu ku makani ihi na utaki niiza ni shanga eligwa nu kumakani ihi nishanga a utaki niiza ni shanga eligwa amaligitilye ku ng'waakwe”
Awa ingi wawo niisusumya, ni itushaa niiza ityataa nsula ni ao niya ubii, ni iketaa nangaluu, naza ku nsailo ao ikongelaa iauya.
Kuiti unyeye, alowa, kumbukiilyi i makani naiza aligitigwe ikali ni alagiiligwa ang'wa Mukulu uYesu kilisto.
Ai aligiilye kitalanyu, “Mu matungo a mpelo yikutula ni antu ni isensa naza ityataa nsula ni yao ni shanga ya weligwa.”
Antu awa ingi atemanuli, ahumeigwe ni nsula ni ya upumoo, hangi agila u ng”wau ng”welu.
Kuiti unyenye, alowa, anga ni mizengaa mu uhuiili nu anyu ni welu nangaluu, ni anga nimilompaa mu ng'wau ng'welu,
ikendegeeli mu ulowa nuang'wa Itunda nu kulindiila u ukende nua Mukulu itu uYesu kilisto niiza wi wikupeza u upanga nua kali na kali.
Lagiili u upolo ku awo niakete u wisinsili. 23
Aguni auya ku kuasapula kupuma mu moto. ku auya lagiili kinya uwai ku woa muze mubipiwe ga nu ng'wenda nuikiwe idoa nu muili.
Itugili ku ng'waakwe nuhumule kumusunja muleke ki kwatya, nu kumusasha mimike ntongeela a ikulyo ni lakwe, tili ubii nu kutula nu ulowa ukulu,
kung'waakwe Itunda wing'wene muguni kukiila uYesu kilisto Mukulu nu itu, ikulyo litule kung'waakwe, ukulu, uhumi, ni ngulu ze ikili i mtungo ihi, ni itungili ga i kali na kali. Amina.
Uwu ukunukuli wang'wa Yesu Kilisto ni Tunda, amupee kualagila itumi akwe imakani nai ibidili apumile, kupipeika. Amu matendile alingike kumutuma umalaika wakwe kumitumi wakwe u Yohana.
U Yohana aupumilye uwihengi nuakila kintu nauine niihusile nulukani lang'wi Tunda nuwihengi naupimigwe kutakilwa nu Yesu Kilisto.
Ukembetilwe wihi nukusoma nukukili nawaehi niakija inkani nuakinyakidagu uu nukukulya aya naandekilwe munu, kunsoko imatungo ahugeela.
Yohana, kumateekelo mupungate nakole kuasia: ukende utule ukole nunyenye nuupolo nupimile kung'wakwe nukoli, naiezukile, hangi nuuziza, hangi kupumila munkolo mupungati niaholi ongeela ni tuntu lakwe ni la utemi.
Hangi kupuma kung'wa Yesu Kilisto nuanso nuuhueli, numuhueli, kutugwa ng'wenso tangi kuawa niakule, hangi mukulu nua mutemi nua mihe eye. kung'waakwe nuanso nuizukuloilwe hangi ukuikile kidesa kupuma mumilandu itu kusakami akwe.
Wakutendile kutula kiutemi imiele ang'wi Tunda hangi nu tataakwe - kung'waakwe kutula ukulu ni ngulu niakale na kale. Huela.
Goza napembya nimalunde; kila iliho likumuona, palung'wi nawa ehi naiamuhomile ni ndogu yehi niyamihe izezee hongelya kung'wakwe ee huela.
Une ni “Alfa hangi Omega,” ulungile umukulu Itunda nuanso nukole hangi niaizukoli, hangi nupembilye, nukete ingulu.
Une, Yohana - muluna ane, hangi niituma palung'we nunyenye munzago hangi muutemi wigigimyeli nuatai nuukole mung'wa Yesu, ainkole mukisiwa kang'wapatimo kunsoko alukani lang'wi Tunda nuwihengi nuutakiwe kung'wa Yesu.
Ainkole kinkolo muluhiku nulamukulu. Ainigule kunyuma nane luli lamigulya anga la talumbeta,
ikalunga, “maandike mumbugulu aya nukumaona hangi umatwale mumatekeelo mupungate, kenda kuaefeso, kenda kuasmilna, kenda kuphiladelphia, hangi nukulaudikia.
Nikapiluka nije luli lang'wa nyenyu naukuligitya nunene naimpilukile nikaona kenara kazahabu kantala mupungate.
Pakatikati akinala kantala aiukoli ung'wi wihangangaa ung'wana nuang'wa Adamu, utugae ngala ndepu aipikile pihe kumigulu akwe, numusipi nua zahabu aiupilimile ikikua.
Itwe lakwe nimasingi akwe ainzelu anga sufu nzelu anga seluji, ni miho akwe aihangangaa ikilimi nula moto.
Impambatilyo yakwe aiyehangangaa ishaba niisile kukila, anga ishaba nakonda kukiiligwa mumoto, nuluhi lakwe ailihangangaa ululi nula mazi nidu nukuluma kwa kukaya.
Aiuambie nzota mupungati mumukono wakwe nuakigoha, nukupumila mumulomo wakwe aukole upanga utaki aikite utaki ubeeli. Uuso wakwe aiukikiliginta anga impasu nintaki.
Nainumuine nikagwa pamigulu akwe anga umuntu nukule. Akaikila umukono wakwe nuwakulila migulya lane nukulunga, “Lekakogopa! Unene nitangi hangi nikwangu.
Hangi nimikie. Ainkulie inge goza, kikie nikali! hangi nkete ifungu niansha nuupanga.
Kuite, maandike numaine, nokole ilungile, naya niikapumila anga aya akila.
Kundogoilyo nipihile munzota mupungati niitakiwe naiuiine mumukono wane nuwakigoha, nikinala kazahabu nikantala mupungate amaileka nimatekeelo mupungate, nikinala nikantala mupungate inge yayo imatekeelo mupungate.
Kung'wa malaika nuitekeelo la kuefeso uandike. Izi inge nkani yang'wa uyu nuambie inzota izo nimupungate munkono wakwe nuwakigoha. Nuanso nuigenda muinala ya zahabu niyantala mupungate ukulungaite.
Ningile nukitendile nikinyangulu kakoni milimo nuigigimieli nuako nuatai kina singaukitendya nao niabe, hangi waagemile ehi niitanga kina atuugwa kumbe singa enso, igeelekile kina ateele.
Ningile kina ulindeie sunga nuigigimieli. Hangi wakieela eedu kunsoko alina lane, hangi kukatala ukile.
Kuite ile lele nilekete kunsoko ako wauleka ulowa wako nuwang'wandyo.
Kuite gwa kimbuka paaugwie wendo uungame hangi nukutenda intendo naiwitenda kupumila ung'wandyo. Angauhite kuungama, nzile kung'wako hangi kukiheja ikindakako kehege pakianza kakwe.
Kuite uewe ukikete ike, umabapewe aya nazaanikolai niomitumile, ga nune numabipiwe.
Anga uze ukete ukutwe, tegeelya aya nung'waung'welu naza akumaila imatekeeelo. Hangi kung'wenso nukumahuma niikamupa ikibali kakulya pikota nilaupanga nuukulu muparadiso nang'wi Tunda.
Kung'wa malaika ukole kitekeelo nilakusmirna uandike izi inge nkani yang'wa uyu nitangi hangi kwangu naukule nukutula mupanga hange.
Ningile ulwago lako hangi nuula wako (ingi ue umugole) nuutele wao niitanga ayahudi (inge singa enso) kumbe isinagogi lang'wa Shetani.
Uleke kogopa ulwago nelekakupata. Goza! Uibilisi uloilwe kumuguma iaoya anyu migeleza nsoko muhime kugeng'wa, hangi mukagigwa mahiku ikumi. Tuli nuuhueli sunga ensha, nii kapuma ingala naupanga.
Ang'wi ukete ukutwe tegeelya ung'waung'welu nukumaila imatekeelo. Nuanso nuwkahuma shangaukupata uube wansha nakabeli.
Kung'wa malaika nuitekeelo la Pargamo andike: Aya yaya nutambue uyu nukete ishenge nikitaki, nukete uwegi ubeele.
Mine ekeanza nuiikie ikaanza nikikole ituntu la utemi nilamulugu. Ga niuu uewe uliambile du ilina lane, hangi shangawaukana uhueli wako nuukule kung'wane, ga nimahiku ayo nang'wa Antipasi mihengi wane, muhueli wane, naubulagilwe mung'wanyu, pang'wanso papo umulugu wikie.
Kuite nkete makani mashenyu kunsokoako, ukete kuang'wanso antu niaambile umanyisigwa nuang'wa Balaamu, nuanso naumumanyisilye Balaki kuika inkigo ntongeela amaisilaeli, uhumile kulya indya niipumigwe isongeelyo kuahing'we nukuulungu.
Mukianza kikokiko, ganue ukete niauyaao niaambile umanyisigwa nua Nikolai.
Ungamagwa! Hangi anguhite kituma ite, kukaya kiza, hangi kuusha mbita kung'wao uwege ukupila mumulomo wane.
Angize ukete ukutwe, tegeelya ung'waung'welu nukulitembula itekeelo. Nuanso nuakadula, niikamupa ga ingwe nilyelu niliandikilwe lina nipya migulya ligwe. Lina nishalimanyilwe ila yuyu nukulisingilya udu.
Kumalaika nuitekeelo lang'wa Thiatira andike. Izi zizi nkani niyang'wi Tunda, nuanso nukete amina akwe anga lulime lamonto, nimpambatilyo anga ishamba nikuluhusiwe kukila.
Ningile ite ikinuitumile ulowa wako nuhueli hangi nukuaelya nuigigimieli nuakowigee, hangi kina ike nukitumile kuupikela inge kukela ike naukitumile pang'wandyo.
Kuite nkete ite ile kunsoko ako umigigimieye umusungu, uyezebeli nuanso nukuitanga munyakidagu nu musungu, kuumanyisi wakwe, ukuakongelaeitumi ane kugoolya. Nukulya indya niipumigwe isongelyo kuwa dudu.
Ainumupee imatungo nuukuungama, kuite shangugombile kuungama uube wakwe.
Goza! Nikaungama mukitanda kandwala nawanituma uusambo nung'wenso mulwago nulutaki, angize shanga uu aungame kuiki naukitumile.
Kuakua ianaao ashe hangi imatekeelo ehi akulinga kina unene nilangaila imasigo ninsula kumupa kila ung'wi wanyu anga intendo yakwe.
Kuite ung'wi anyu numusague mu Thiatira, kuawa ehi nishaambile umanyisigwa uwu, hangi nishaamumanyile iki niang'wi itanga umanyisigwa amulugu, kulunga kitalanyu, singa kuika muligo wihi migulya lanyu.
Kikani lehi, yemupasile mutule muakomu sunga ninikasuka.
Wehi nuikadula nukituma ike nainitumile kupikiila sunga impeelo, kung'waako nuanso uhumi mundugu.
Ukumutawaala, kumulanga nuashuma, anga mabakuliaulole wikamubunanga ininoinino.
Nu nene nikaminkiilya inzota iyo na ki daudau.
Angeze ukite ukutwi legeelya eke nung'waung'welu nukumatambuila imatekeelo
Kung'wa malaika witekeelo lakusardi, yang'wa yuyu nuambie inkolo izo nimupungate niyang'wi Tunda ni nzota mpungate. Nungile ike nuitumile ukete lukumo kina umupanga, kuite ukule.
Uka uzipilye nasagie, kuite akole pakupi kusha kunsoko singaniine intendo yako ikondaniie pamiho nang'wi Tunda wane.
Kuite, kembuka, naumasigiye nukija magombe nukila ituma. Ite anguhite kuuka, nzile anga umuhimbi, hangi shanga ukulinga itungo nileule ninikiza kung'waako.
Kuite akole mina mashenyi naantu musardi niang'wi shangaiashapue inguo yao. Akugenda palung'wi nunene, atugae inguo nzelu, kunsoko agombilwe.
Nuanso niakuhuma wikakumbwa ngala ni nzelu, hangikwee, shangakuliheja ilina lakwe kupuma mumbugulu naupanga, hangi kulita elina lakwe ntongeela ang'wa Tata wane hange ntongeela amalaika.
Angeze ukete ukutwe, tegeelya ung'waung'welu nukung'wa malaika nuitekeelo.
Kung'wa malaika nuitekeelo, kung'wa philadelfia andeke. Nkani naiya mtakatifu nitai - nukete ifunguo yang'wa Daudi, wilugula hangi kutile nukulugaila, wilugaila hangi kutile nuhumile kulugula.
Ningile ike nuikitumile. Goza nukuikiiye ntongeela ako mumulango nulugue inge kutile nuhumile kuulugula. Ningile ukete ngulu nshenyi, ite ugombile ulukani lane hangi shawakana ilina lane.
Goza! Ehi niakole misinagogi nilamulugu, awa niilunga ayahudi kumbe singa enso, kumbe ekongelana. Niikaatenda aze akusujudu ntongeela amigulu ako, hangi ekalinga kina ainukuloilwe.
Kunsoko utunzile ilago lane ikizewigigimieye kutai, kusunga ganimatungo ako nakugeng'wa ayo napembilye muunkumbigulu wihi, kuagema awa ehi niakee mihe.
Kukaya kiza. Ambeela kukila eke inge watule kutile umuntu nukuhegelya ingala ako.
Niikamutenda uyu nukuma kutula kimpandwa mitekeelo lang'wi Tunda wane, lina lakisale kang'wi Tunda wane (Yerusalemu mpya, nukusima pihe kupumiila kilunde kung'wa kilunde kung'wi Tunda wane), nelina lane ipya.
Uyu nukete ukutwi, nuije ehi nung'waung'welu nukulunga kumatekeelo.
“Kung'wa malaika nuitekeelo nilakulaudikia andike: Kunkani yakwe nuanso numuhueli, nuakutegemelwa hangi mukueli numuhueli, mutemi nuaunkumbigulu nawang'wi Tunda.
Mine kihi nukitumile, hangi singa uewe singawiampeepuang'wi singa wimupyu, nsumbiye kina wizatula wiampepo ang'wi wimupyu.
Ite, kunsoko uewe umupyupyu singa umupyu ang'wi wiampepo, kuluuka upume mukilakala kane.
Kunsoko ukulinga, “Une ninungile, nukutula ninsao yedu hangi singandoilwe kehi.” Kuite shangaulingile kina uewe umuula kukele, umukia, umuhembi mupoku nuikwepwa.
Tegeelya nukusegye une: Gula kung'wane ezahabu nogigwe numoto ite ulije ugole niang'wenda nielo niakumiligenta. Ite wikumbe ulekekigeelya iminyala akipwi kako, nimakula naiwipaka muilomo ako uhume kuona.
Wehi ninumuloilwe, nimulagila nukumumanyisa ninonee kikie kuite gwa, tula wiatai nukuungama.
Goza nimekile pamulango nukuupendola. Wihe nukija ululi lane nukumulugwila umulango, kupembya nukingila munyumbakwe, nukulya indya nung'wenso, nung'wenso palung'wi nunene.
Nuanso nuikahuma, kumupa itai kikie pihe palung'wi nunene pigulya lituntu nilautemi, anga unene nainihumile nikikie pihe palung'wi nutata wane pigulya lintuntu nilautemi.
Uyu nukete ukutwi, nuwije eke nung'waung'welu ukumaila imatekeelo.
Naiakee imakani aya nikagoza, nikaona kina umulango auluguwe kilunde. Ulo uloli lang'wandyo, ikaze ligitya nunene anga itarumbeta, ikalunga nzi kunu, kuulagila aya niikapumila angakela imakani aya.
Nkua eng'wi ainkale ikinkolo, aimine aikole ni tuntu lautemi leikilwe kilunde, numuntu ulikaie.
Ung'wi naulikae aiwigee anga igwe nila yasipi niakiki. Aiukole nuuta nuambula aiupilimiye ituntu nilautemi. Uuta nua mbula awigee anga zumaridi.
Kulipilimikilya ituntu la utemi aiakole imatuntu autemi nimangiza ishilini nanne, hangi aikie matuntu autemi aikie ianyampala ishilini nanne, akumbilwe ang'wenda elu ni ngala sahabu mumatwe ao.
Kupumila mituntu lautemi aipumile nzahe nialopito, numugugumo nulupeto ntala mupungate aiyakiee ntonge ela ituntu la utemi, ntala ainkulu mupungate yang'wi Tunda.
Hangi ntongeela ituntu lautemi aikole mpola, aigee anga ikioo. Ehi kupumila ituntu lautemi aikole niakete upanga anne, naiizoe imiho kuntongeela nukunyumba.
Keambe nikang'wandyo ukete upanga welu anga ung'wang'ombe, kumbe nuakatatu ukete upanga akete uusu anga umuntu, nuyu nukete upanga nuaka ne aiihanganga inde nilumile.
Iumbe ine niikete upanga kila ung'wiao aukete manana mutandatu, izue imiho migulya nipihe akwe. Utiku numung'wi shaikilaga kulunga, ukulu, ukulu, numukulu Itunda mutemi nuaintu yehi, naizukole nuyu naukole hangi nuyu nuzizeza.
Kila imatungo iumbe nikete upanga aipumilye ukulu, ikulyo nuulumbi ntongeela ang'wa uyu naiwikie mituntu nilautemi, nuanso nukie kalinikali.
Ianyampala makumi abeeli, aiaminamie ienso ntongeela ang'wa akwe naulikae ituntu la utemi. Aiatunile pihe pang'wakwe nuikie ikale nikale nukulunga.
Uewe ustahile muukulu witu ni Tunda witu kusingilya ululu nikulyo ningulu. Kunsoko auiumbile iintu yehi hangi anga nuloilwe uewe, aiakole hangi aiaumbilwe.
Hangi nikaona mukono wakwe nuakulila nuang'wa uyu naiwikie mituntu la utemi, gomba naileandekilwe kuntongela nukunyuma, hangi ailekete ugomola mupungati.
Ainumuine malaika aukete ingulu akizetanantya kukila nalukulu, nyanyu nuyumunonee kulugula igombo nukubunanga uugomola wakwe.
Kutile anga muntu kilunde ang'we muunkumbigulu ang'we kuulungu nauuhumile kulugula igombo ang'we kusoma.
Aindeile kuawa kunsoko, singaaiwigee wehi naiyemunonee kulugula ang'we kulesoma.
Kuite ung'we waa anyampala wikambila “Leka kulila. Goza! ihimba naendogu ang'wa Yuda, itina lang'wa Daudi, udoile, hangi uhumile kulelugula igombo nuugomola wakwe numupungati.”
Kate naituntu la utemi nawanipanga anne niang'we anyampala, aimine ng'wankolo akizewimikile, akizewigee anga ubunangilwe. Aukete mpembe mupungate ni miho mupungate izi inge nkolo mupungate niyang'wi Tunda niitumilwe muunkumbigulu wehi.
Wikalongola wakahola igombo kupumila mumukono wakwe nuakigoha nuang'wa uyu naiwikie mituntu lautemi.
Pina wikahola igombo, nilaupanga wanne nianyampala, makumi abiile nuune ikatuna pihe ntongeela ang'wa nkolo. Kila ung'waao akete nikinubi nibakuli la zabibu nilizue uuvumba nanso malompi auhueli.
Aekemba wembo upya. Unonee kuhola igombo nukulugula ugomola wakwe. Kunsoko ausenzilwe nukusakami wakwe akamuguilya Itunda eantu akila ndogu, ntambu niashenyi mihe.
Wikaatenda atemi hangi atongeeli akumitumila Itunda itu, akulema migulya lehi.
Hangi nikagoza nukija nduli yamalaeka edu kupilimikilya ituntu lautemi eidadi ao ai 200,000,000 nawa niapanga nianyampala.
Ikalunga kululi, “Unonee ung'wankolo nausenzilwe kusengelya uhumi, ugole, upolo, ngulu, ikulyo, ukulu, nukukuligwa.
Nikakija kehi naikiumbilwe naikikole kilunde numu unkimbigulu numukate niihe numigulya na bahali, kela ikintu kikazelunga, “Kung'waakwe nuanso nuikie mituntu lautemi nukung'wankolo, kutula lukumo, ikulyo, ukulu ni ngulu niakulema ikali na kali.”
Niaupanga anne ikalunga, “Huela! “ nianyampala ikatuma pihe nukukulya.
Nikagoza imatungo ung'wankolo naulugue ung'wi nuaugomola eyi nemupungate, nikija ung'we ao niapanga anne akazelunga, kululi nulipyani nulupito, “Nzuu!”
Nikagoza aikoli falasi nzelu! Naumunankie aukete ibakuli hangi wikapegwa ngala. Aeupumie anga umuduli nuduli nsoko wadule.
Imatungo ang'wankolo nautugue ugomola wakabeele nikija nuaupanga nuakabeeli wikalunga nzuu!
Hangi efalasi ninzuya akigela nkauku anga umoto nauninkae augombigwe kuheja upolo muunkumbigulu, kina iantu isinze. Uyu naumunankie aupewe shege nikitaki.
Imatungo ang'wankolo nautugue uugomola uo nuuakatatu nikija nuwaupanga nuakatatu wikalunga, “Nzuu!” Nekaona falasi nzelu, hangi nauminankie aukete ngele mumukono wakwe.
Nikija ululi nailigeleekile kung'we wao niakete upanga wikalunga, “kebaba kangano nidinali ing'wi. Kuite uleke kumakanza imakuta na divai.”
Imatungo ung'wankolo naulugue uugomola wakane, nikija ululi la awa nianne ikalunga, “Nzuu!”
Hangi nikaona efalasi akijivu. Nauminankie aukitangwa elina lakwe nsha, nukuulungu aimutyatie aupewe uhumi migulya a nkolo niamihe, kubulaga kukiila shege, kunzila, nukulwala, nukuikale yamihaka niamihe.
Imatungo ang'wa nkolo nautugue ugomola wakataano, aimine pihe pakizindalo inkolo yao awa naiabulagilwe, kunsoko alukani lang'wi Tunda hangi kulinga uwihengi naiauambile kutai.
Ikalela kululi nulukulu, “kupuma nale, mutemi waintu yehi, mtakatifu ni tai wikaalamula neikie migulya ehi nukumikomolya isakami itu?
Hangi kila ung'we ao aupewe mujolungu ng'welu hangi wikailwa kina inonee kulindila inino sunga nuekakondanila ualigwa nuukondile nuaitumi auya nialuna ao niasungu nawa niagoha niikakondanila nikabulagwa, anga uu nianso naiabulagilwe.
Imatungo ung'wankolo naulugue ugomola wamutandatu nijagoza hangi ailikole itetemeko ikulu. Ilyoa likatula ilwalu pii anga igonila la singa, nung'weli wehi wikatula anga isakami.
Inzota yakilunde yekagwa pihe, anga ikota nilelagalya inkali yakwe matungo ampepo nuehingisigwa nukimpupu.
Anga likahega anga igombo nilipingilitigwe. Kila umulima ni siwa aiihegigwe mahali pakwe.
Hangi iatemi ehi niantu alukumo ni ajemedari, agole, nianulu, hangi kila ung'wiao naimutungwa nuwidesile u akipiha mumakulungu nimumagwe numumagulu.
Ikamaila imalugulu nimagwe, “Kulugweeli! Kupihi pa usowakwe uyu nuiwikie pituntu lautemi nukupima muulaki.
Kunsoko eye nuluhiku nulukulu nulaulaki wao wahugiila, hangi inge nyanyu nuhumile kimeka.
Kukila udu aya nikaona malaika anne imekile munindo inne niyehi, aiagiiye eahing'wi anne niamihe kungulu kunsoko inge ang'wega itule kutile mihe, migulya mubahali ang'wi mikota lehi.
Nikaona numalaika umuya akeza kupuma kilya, naukete ugomola wang'wi Tunda numupanga. Akalila kulili lukulu kuamalaika anne naeagombigwe kubepya ehinibahali.
“Muleke kubepya ehi, bahali ang'wi makota sunga panga kueka uugomola muusu mumatwe aitumi ang'wi Tunda witu.”
Nikija utimili wa awa naiaikilwe ugomola, 144,000 naiaikilwe ugomola kupuma kila ndugu naantu aislaeli.
12,000 kupuma mundugu aya Yuda niaekilwe ugomola, 12,000 kupuma mundugu ang'wa Rubeni, 12,000 kupuma mundugu ang'wa Gadi.
12,000 kupuma mundugu ang'wa Asheli, 12,000 kupuma mundugu ang'wa Naftali, 12,000 kupuma mundugu ang'wa Manase.
12,000 kupuma mundugu ang'wa Simioni, 12,000 kupuma mundugu ang'wa Lawi, 12,000 kupuma mundugu ang'wa Isakari.
12,000 kupuma mundugu ang'wa Zabuloni, 12,000 kupuma mundugu ang'wa Yusufu hangi 12,000 kupuma mundugu ang'wa Benjamini naukuilwe uugomola.
Anga kila imakani aya, nikagoza, aiikole iiumbe ikulu kutile umuntu nuhumile kuiilya kupuma kilaihe, ndogu nejamaa nintambu - imekile ntongeela ituntu la utemi hangi ntongeela ang'wa nkolo. Aiatugae amujulungu elu hangi aiakete nimatambe amitende mumikono ao.
Hangi aiakitanga kululi lamigulya: “Uuguni wang'wi Tunda nuikie mituntu lautemi, nukung'wankolo.
Iamalaika ehi aiemekile kupilima ituntu lautemi hangi kuapilima eanyampala ao palung'wi nao niaupanga anne, akaluma pihe, nihe hangi ikaika uusu migulya nihe ntongoela ituntu lautemi hangi ikamukulya itunda.
Ikalunga “Huela, Kulya, upolo, ilumbi, ikulyo, uhumi ni ngulu yang'wi Tunda witu ikale nikale. Huela.”
Hangi ung'wi wao nuanyampala wikakankolya, “awa anyenyu niatugae eamijolungu nielu, hange apumile pe?
Wikambela, “Bwana mukulu, ulengile uewe,” wikambila hangi, awa wawa niapumile mulwango nulukulu ile iamejolongo ao nukuitenda nzelu kusakami ang'wankolo.
Kunsoko eye, akole ntongeela ituntu lautemi nilang'wi Tunda hangi akumukulya ung'wenso utiko numung'we mitekeelo lakwe.
Shanga akuona inzala hangi, sunga ni nyota hangi. Ilyoa shangalikuansonsa, sunga upyu nuakusonsa.
Kunsoko ung'wankolo nukole pakatekate nituntu lautemi mudemi wao, hangi wikaatongeela munjilyo ya maze, ni Tunda wikaapyagula uliholi mumiho ao.
Imatungo ang'wankolo naulugue uugomola nuwamupungate, yekatula ihetwe kilunde pakupe enusu saa.
Hange nikaona iamalaika mupungate imekile ntongela ang'wi Tunda, ekapegwa tarumbeta mupungate.
Wekiza numuya umalaika, uambie ibakuli la zahabu lekete uvumba, wimikile pakizindaalo. Wekapegwa uuvumba nuuya kunsoko ite apumie palung'wi nimalompi auhueli ehi pakizindaalo nikazambalau ntongeela intuntu lautemi.
Ulyoki nulauvumba, palung'we nimalompi auhueli, lukanonenkela migulya ntongela ang'wi Tunda kupuma mumukono wang'wa malaeka.
Umalaeka nilauvumba ibakuli nilauvumba weki zezulya umoto. umoto kupuma pakizindaalo. Hangi wikalegoma pihe migulya nihe, hangi yekapumila induli niampeto, nzahi niyampito nimatetemo nihe.
Awo eamalaika nimupungate niakete impembe mupungate ekatula akondile kuikua.
Umalaika nuang'wandyo wikamikua impembe akwe, ikapumila mbula amagwe numoto nuhalinkanile nusakami. Ikagung'wa pihe muunkumbigulu inge niang'we apyee, imakota ang'we nimafu nimatotu ikapya.
Umalaika nuakubeele akakua impembe akwe, nekentuanga umulima nuukulu naukupya numumoto ukagung'wa mubahali. Ipande nilabahali lekatula sakami.
iintu ing'wi niipanga niyamubahali yekasha, nimeli inzuya yekabipa.
Umalaika nuwakatatu wikakua impembe akwe, ninzota nkulu ekagwa kupuma kilunde, ikazeemelekile angaitoshi migulya amumyongo ing'wi ao ninjilyo niyamaze.
Elina nilanzota aipakanga. Imaze nang'we ekatula pakanga, neantu edu ekasha kunsoko amaze naimalulu.
Umalaika nuakane wikakua impembe akwe, ipande la lyoa lekakuwa, palung'wi palung'wi nipande lang'weli ni nzota ing'wi yao gaa. Kuite ipande laintu izi yapiluka kutula kiti hangi ipande, theluthi amung'we nitheluthi autiku aekutile anga welu.
Aingozile, hangi nikija inde nailumile umo migulya, akizitanga kululi lukulu, “Ukia, ukia, ukea kuawa neikie mihe, kunsoko akutumbwa nimpembe niisagie inge ahugeela kukuwa numalaika wakatatu.
Hangi umalaika wakatano wakakua empembe akwe. Nikaona nzota kupuma kilunde naigwie munu mihe inzota ikapegwa uluguli wikombo nililongoe mikombo nigila anga mpelo.
Wikalugula ikombo nigila anga mpelo, nulyoki likanankela migulya lakazelipangile kupuma mukate nikombo anga elyoki nulupimile mitanulu nikulu. Ilyoa nugulya yekakaeleka yekatula kiti kunsoko alyoki naelukupuma mikombo.
Mukate mikombo ingaga yekapuma keza migulya namihe nienso aiapewe ingulu anga zizi niyankume niamigulya ehi.
Aeaiwe aleke kubipya emafa, na mihe ang'wi umumea wehi nuutotu ang'wi ikota, inge eantu du nishanga akuilwe uugomola wang'wi Tunda muntongeela ausu wao.
Shangaiagombigwe kuabulaga iantu nianso, kuaja udu kunyeeli eataano. Uwai wao ai anga wuwu nuwakulung'wa inkume niimuluma umuntu.
Mumahiku nanso eantu akumiduma ensha, inge shang akumelija. Akulija ensula nakusha, inge ensha ekumanka.
Ingaga aiyempyani nefalasi neinonee igwe kumbita mumatwe aikete kintu anga ngala nazahabu nukuusu ai hanga iantu.
Aiakite imasingi anga iazungu nimino ao aiehanganga nihimba.
Aiakete ikua angaikua yayuma ni ndoli niyamaba ao aihanganga. Ululi nulamagale nidu nambita nifalasi niyukumanka kulongola kumbita.
Aiakete imekila nikeluma anga enkume mumekila ao aiekole ingulu niakubepya eantu kumyeli ataano.
Aeakole nung'wenso anga mutemi migulya ao malaika nuwamikombo nigila empelo. Elina lakwe iikieblania inge Abadoni, ekeyunani ukete lina Apolioni.
Ukia nuang'wandyo wakila. Goza! anga ile lakela uzile hangi ukia wakabeele.
Umalaika nuamutandatu wikakua impembe akwe, nikija ululi lupumie panindo akizindaalo nikole ntongeela ang'wi Tunda.
Ululi lukamuila umalaika nuamutandatu naukete impembe, “Alekele iamalaika anne niatungilwe mumongo mumongo nuukulu nua afrati.
Iamalaika anne aiaikilwe kumatungo yayo ikulu, uluhiku nulanso, nung'weli nuanso, nung'waka nuanso, ailekewe aabulage iaoya ao niantu.
Utimili nuaikui aiamole migulya afalasi aiakole 200,000,000. Nikija utimeli nuao.
Eti inge uu azamine ifalasi mundoti yane nawa naiamankie migulya ao. Ikua yao aiikauku anga umoto, bluu niye niyelu niisheeye. Imatwe afalasi aimpyani ni matwe nihimba, numumilomo ao aiupumile moto, lyoki ni salfa.
Antu ang'wi ekabulagwa ni mapigo aya natatu, moto, nisalfa naipumile mumilomo ao.
Kunsoko ingulu afalasi aikole mumilomo ao mumikela ao - kunsoko imekela ao aihanganga inzoka, hangi aiakete imatwe naiamitumie kuika inkomele muantu.
Eantu niasagile, awa nisinga aiabulagilwe nimapigo aya, shaikaungama kuntendo yao naitumile, hangeshaikaleka kukulya iahing'wi niadudu nia zahabu, hela, shaba, magwe nimakota - maintu nishamuhumile kumaona, kija kang'wi kugenda.
Hangi shaikaungama ubulagi wao, ulogi wao, nuukosi wao ang'wi ninzila yao niyawii.
Hangi nikaona malaika numuya numukulu akizesima pihe kupuma kilunde. Aeutungilwe milunde hangi aiukole utaa nuambula mitwe lakwe. Usuu wakwe aiwihanganga ilyoa, ni migulu akwe aie ihanganga ikepandwa moto.
Aiuambie igombo ninino mumukono niailelugue, ung'we auuikile umugulu wakwe nuwakuliela migulya amubahali numugulu wakwe nuwankege migulya lihe ninyumu.
Hangi wikitunta ululi lamigolya anga ihimba nimatungo naiwituntile kululi mpito mupungate yekakuamika.
Imatungo impito mupungate naikwanukile, ainahugeela kuandika, kuite nikija ululi kupumila kilunde likezelunga, “Sunga itule kinkunku ehi nimpito mupungate. Usiandike.”
Hangi umaleika nainumuine wimikile migulya amubahali numihe ni nyumu, auhumbue umokono wakwemigulya milunde
nukulapa kung'wa uyu nuikie ikale na kale nauumbile ilunde naya ehi nakole, unkumbigolo naya ehi, hange bahali naya ehi nakole: “Ikakutile hange.
Kuite kuluhiku nulanso, imatungo aamalaika mupungate nuamalaika nuekahugeela kukua impembe akwe, kuite uakunku wang'wi Tunda ekawakonda, anga nutanantilye kuitumi akwe eanyakidagu.”
Ululi nainigule kupuma milunde lekambela hangi longola, hola igombo nininao nailigeeigwe nilekole mumukono wang'wa malaeka naiwimekile migulya abahali mumihe ninyumu.
Hangi nikalongola kung'wa malaika nukumuela wampe igombo nininoo. Wikambela, “Hola igombo ulye lekamitenda enda etule nuwai, kuite mumulomo nuako lekatula lemulyo anga uuke.”
Nikahola igombo inino kupuma mumulomo nuane, kuite anga nalya enda nane ekatula auwai.
Hangi induli ing'we yekambela, “Yekunonee utabili hange kuantu needu, mahe, ndogu niatemi”
Aimpegilwe nawanzi nukutula anga mulanga nuakugemeelya. Aembewe. “Itega hangi genda ugemelye itekeelo lang'wi Tunda nekezindaalo. nawaniakukulya mung'wanso.
Kuite uleke kugemeelya ekeanda kakunzi nekitekeelo kunsonko apegilwe antu nianyakelungu, ekalita ekesale nikitakatifu kumatungo angw'eli makumi anne nuubeele.
Nikaapa ahueli anne abeele uhumi nuakutabili kumatungo amahiku 1260, ekaatugae emagunila.
Iahueli awa inge makota abeele namizeituni nemenala ebeele nimekile ntongeela amukulu nuaunkumbigulu.
Anga muntu wehi ukulamula kuazulu, umoto wepume ela mumilomo ao nukuazulu ialugu ao. Wehi nukulowa kuazulu ukusinja kubulagwa kunzila yeye.
Eahueli awa akete uhumi nuakulugaila ilunde ingeembula eleke kukua imatungo niakutabili. Akete ingulu niakukailwa imaze, atule sakami nukumikua ihe kukila imampilu nipigo imatungo ehi nialoilwe.
Imatungo angapike amale uwihengi nuao, ekekale kehi kekupuma mikombo nigila empelo akituma embita nianso akuahuma nukuabulaga.
Emeeli ao ekulala mumutaa nuwakesale nekekulu kumpani ukitangwa Sodoma ni Misili, pang'wanso umukulu nuao autumbekilwe.
Kumahiku atatu nenusu ang'wi ekapuma muanluu ntambu, kabila hange kila itaifa akugoza emeele ao hange shakupumya kuekwa mukebeela.
Awa neakie mihe akulowa kunsoko ao nukulumbeelya, sunga akipa nizawadi kunsoko anyakidagu neabeele aagilye awa naeakole mihe.
Kuite anga yakela nsiku itatu ninusu imehupo naupanga kupuma kung'wi Tunda ekigeela neenso akimeka kungulu ao. Akutula nuukulu awa niakuaona.
Hangi akija luli lukulu kupuma kilunde akuaela, nzii kunu, “nianso ekalongola migulya kulikalo milunde neansoealugu ao ekaagozee.
Musaa nanso ikalekole itetemeko ikulu nelihe eng'wi amumahe ikumi, Ekagwaw. Antu elfu mupungate akubulagwa nimatetemeko nao niakusaga apanga akogopa mupa Itunda nuakilunde uukulu.
Uukea wakabeele wakela; Goza uukea nuwakatatu upembilye ukaiye.
angi umalaeka nuamupungate wikakua impembeakwe, ninduli nkulu yekatambula kilunde nukulunga. Uutemi nuamihe wainautemi wamukulu wehi hange wang'wa Kilisto nuakwe. ukutema ekale nakale.
Hangi anyampala makumi abeele nune aiikie mituntu nilautemi, ntongeela ang'wi Tunda aiagwie ienso pihe mulonkunde, nuuso wao aiukunamile nienso ekamukulya Itunda.
Ikangi, “Kupumya esongeelyo litu kung'wankolo mukulu Itunda mutemi waintu yehi naukole nuyu nukole, kunsoko wahola engulu yako nukanza kutemya.
Ianyakilungu ikataka, kuite ikuo lako lazaa imatungo akapika iashi kulamula nuewe kuapokela eitumi ako enyakedagu, ehueli nawa niakete uwoa nua lina lako. Ehi niabeele singaawezilye anga kentu awa nianyangulu. Nimatungo ako apika nakuabuya awa naebepya ihe.
Hangi itekeelo lang'wi Tunda nuakilunde lekalugulwa nisandiko lawigombyi nuakwe likigela nitekeelo lakwe. Aiikole nzahi ya welu, mugugumo wampeto, itetemeko lihe nimagwe ambula.
Kelingasiilyo kekulu kekigela kung'wanso kilunde musungu nauambilwe ni iyoa, akezeukete nung'weli pihe pamigulu akwe, nengala nanzota ikumi, ing'wi nuubele migulya mitwe lakwe.
Aukete uube hange ukeze lela kunsoko auai wakutuga muupyu wakitunguiela.
Nikiuya kilingasiilyo kekigela kilunde, Goza! Yikatula ikole nzoka kauku nkulu ekete matwe mupungate ni mpembe ikumi, hange aikole ngala mupungate mumatwe ao.
Umukela wakwe aiulutie ipande la nzota kilunde nukuigoma pihe muunkumbigulu. Inzoka akimeka ntongeela amasungu naiwahugeela kutuga, inge anga imatungo akutuga, emumele ung'wakwe ao.
Aulungile ng'wana, mung'enya wakigoha, nuakatema imahe ehi kumulanga nuashuma umung'enya wakwe wekapulwa migulya kung'wi Tunda hange kituntu lakwe nilautemi.
Numusungu wikamanka mumbuga, ekianza nekanso Itunda aiwanonelya pang'wanso kunsoko akwe, inge wahume kualigwa mahiku 1,260.
Itungo yekatula nembita kilunde. Mikaeli niamalaeka akwe, ekikua nenzoka pihe niamalaeka akwe akikua nuyo.
Kuite inzoka aigila anga ngulu yakukondya kudula inge gwa yekatula kutile ilyoma hange kilunde kunsoko akwe niamalaeka akwe.
Izoka nikulu enzoka iyo nakale nitangwe ibilisi ang'wi Shetani nuekongela - ihe wikagung'wa pihe mihe niamalaika akwe ekagung'wa pihe palung'wi nuyo.
Hangi nekija luli lukulu kupuma kilunde: “Itungeele ugunwa wazaa, ngulu, nuutemi wang'wi Tunda witu nuuhumi wang'wa Kilisto nuakwe. Kunsoko umusemi nualuna ehi wagung'wa pihe - naeuasemee ntongeela ang'wi Tunda witu utiko numung'we.
Aeamusemee kusakami ang'wankolo nukulukani lawihengi nuao, kundogoelyo shangaealoilwe ulikalo laosunga ensha.
Kuite lumbeelyi, unye kilunde, hange ehi neikie neikie mukate akwe. Kuite ukia wehi nibahali kunsoko umulugu wasima kung'waanyu. Wizue ikuo nitaki, kunsoko ulengile kina ukete matungo mashenyidaa.
Imatungo izoka, naeleine kina lagung'wa pihe wikamutyata umusungu naiwitugile ung'wana numugoha.
Kuite umusungu wekapegwa manana ande abeele makulu, kuitegwa ahume kuluma nukupika pang'wanso nainoneigwe kunsoko akwe kuko kumbuga, keanza nekanso kekumile kumusunga, kumatungo, matungo nanusu matungo, kianza nishalehumile kupika izoka nelanso.
I nzoka ikahunula emaze kupuma mumulomo wakwe anga umoto, inge alete ekarika nakukapilya.
Kuite ihe ekamuaelya umusongu, ekamaha umulomo wakwe nukuumila umongo ulewe nizoka kupumila kumulomo wakwe.
Hangi izoka likamutakila umusungu nuyo wikahenga nukituma embita kuutugwa wakwe wehi - kuawa niagombile imalago ang'wi Tunda nukuambela wihengi nuang'wa Yesu.
Izoka lekimeka hange migulya amehanganga muluguo la bahali.
Hange nekaona kekale kekapuma mubahali. Aieukete mpembe ikumi nimatwe mupungate. Mumpembe yqkwe aikole ngala ikumi numitwe lakwe aeikole nkani.
Eke ikakale nainukiine inge anga ihue. Emegulu akwe anga edubu, numulomo wakwe anga ihimba izoka ile lekamupa ingulu, numituntu lakwe nilautemi nuhumi nuangulu kukela nukutema.
Itwe lakekale king'wi kao iekigeeleka kutula ninkomele nkulu naizesasha inshakwe. Kuite inkomele akwe akapola, nihe ehi ikakuelwa nukukityata ikekale.
Hangi ikalikulya izoka ndogoelyo kekapegwa uhumi ekekale eke. Ikakekulya ekekale kwe, hange ekalongoleka kulunga; nyenyu anga kekale? hange nyenyu nukikua neko?
Ikekale kekapegwa melomo ketambule inkani yakikulya nukutukila. Aeugombigwe kutula nuuhumi kumyeli makumianne nuubeele.
Kuite ikekule kikamaha umulomo wakwe nukuligitya ituki kumutukila itunda, akaletukila elina lakwe, pang'wanso naewikie nawa neikie kilunde.
Ekekale kekapegwa lyoma kituma mbita neahueli nukuahuma, hange wekapegwa uhumi kikila ekabila, antu, ntambu, nihe.
Eehi neikie muunkumbigulu akumukulya nuanso kukela ung'weao elina lakwe nesingalandekilwe, kupuma ihe nauumbewe, mumbugulu naupanga, inge nekang'wankolo, nausensilwe.
Angeze ukole wehi nukete ukutwe uategeelye.
Angeze ung'weao uhoilwe utugwa, nukutugwa winzu. angeze ung'weao ukubulaga kushege, kushege kiko ukubulagwa, uwu witangwi nuaupolo hange wigigimyeeli kuawa niatakatifu.
Hange nikaona kekale nekiuya kepembilye kupuma mihe. Aekekete mpembe ibeele anga enkolo hange kekaligitya anga izoka.
Wikalageela uhumi wehi kukekale eke nekang'wandyo nuukole wakwe, nukituma mehi nawa neikie mung'wanso, kukulya ekekale nekanso nikang'wandyo, uyu nenkomeleakwa aipoile.
Wikituma makula du, sunga wikautenda umoto wikasima pihe kupuma kilunde wikigela ntongeela aantu.
Kilengaseelyo augombigwe kituma, wikaakongela awaneikie mihe, akazeaela azipye eadudu kikulyo lakikale naekelemaigwe kuwege, kuite kekili kukikie.
Aiugombigwe kupumya emihupo kung'wa dudu kekali kehume kutambula nukusasha awa ehi niahitile kukulya ekekale abulagwe.
Hange wikasinja kukila ung'we ao, numugila ensailo, nuyu nuangulu, mugole numuhimbe, nuidesile numutugwa kusengeelya ugomola kumokono wakigoha ang'wi nuusu wao.
Inge shangaeagombekile kuhela muntu kugulya ang'wi kugula, inge kusinja wezeukete ugomola nuanso hangi nelina lakekale nikanso ang'wi ulimeeli nualina lakwe.
Pang'wanso papo ukole uupolo. Nuanso nuukete eemahala, nuaelye utimeli nuakekale eke, ndogoelyo naewitumile nuakiuntu. Nuutimeli wakwe inge namba 666.
Nikagoza hange nikaona ng'wankolo winaekile ntongeela ane migulya mulugulu nula sayuni. Paalung'wi nung'wenso ai 144,000 naeakete elina lakwe nelina lakwe utata akwe ailiandekilwe kuntongeela nuusu nuao.
Nikija ululi kupuma kilunde aiekijika anga mululumo nua mazi nedu nululi lukulu nulalupeto. Ululi naenigule inge anga iekua impembe yao.
Ikazemba wimbo upya ntongeela nituntu lautemi hange ntongeela ao awa niakete upanga neanne nianyampala. Kutile anga nuauhumi nuakumanya uwimbo nuanso inge wawadu 144,000 niakomowe kupumila mihe.
Awa wawa nisingangaa ikanzile ienso kuasungu, kundogoilyo aisungile ienso kuntendo yausambo, Inge wawa naiamutytile ung'wankolo pehi naekeze nkali yang'wandyo kung'wi Tunda hange nukung'wankolo.
Kutile anga utele naeutambuwe mumilomo ao shangaiemeilwe.
Nikamuona malaeka numuya akazewimekile mumalunde, naukete impola niyakilunde kunkani ninza kuatanatelya neikie mihe kukela ihe, ndugu, nambu niantu.
Wikaitanga kululi nulukulu, “mugopi Itunda hangi mupi uukulu. Kundogoilyo ematungo auamuli ahugela. Mukuli ung'wenso, nuanso nijeelyo yamaziwa.
Malaeka numungeza - malaeka wakabiile - wikatyata wikalunga, “Ugwie - ugwie Babeli nuukulu, nuang'wensilye ianyakilungu imagae naukosi, megaenanso ikaleta utaki kung'waakwe.
Malaeka numungeza - malaeka wakatatu wekaatyata wikalunga kululi, “Nulukulu wihi nuekakulya ekekale nekanso nududu wakwe, nukusingilya ugomola kuntongeela ausu wakwe kang'wi kumukono.
Nung'wenso ga ukung'wa imagae nautaki wang'wi Tunda imagai nanso aeazipegwa nukukunulwa singaeahalinkanigwe nikikombe kautaki wakwe. Umtunuekang'wa ukagigwa numoto hange numoto nuakebiliti ntongela amalaeka akwe niakuigwe hange btongeela ang'wankolo.
Nulyuki nulaube wao ukalongola ikale nekale hange agila anga kusupya mong'we ang'wi utiku awa neekolya ikekale nudubu wakwe, hange kila umuntu nuusingeye ugomola nualina lakwe.
Uu witangwi wakulindela nukigigimelya kuakueli awa neze amagombile imalago ang'wi Tunda nuuhueli wang'wa Yesu.
Aigule ululi kupuma milunde ekalunga, “Andekeaya; Bahu eashi neashie kung'wa Bwana, “Ee” alungile ung'waung'welu, “wahume kusupya kupumela mumikomo ao, indogoilyo intendo yao nukuatyata.”
Aingozile nikaona ailekole ilunde lyelu, hange naewikie milunde aiung'wi aewipyani nung'wana witu. Aukete engala azahabu mitwe lakwe numuundu utaki mumukono wakwe.
Malaeka mungeza wakeza hange kupuma mitekeelo hange wikitanga kululi lukenda kung'wa uyu naiwikie milunde: Hola umuundu wako wandye kuogola. Kunsoko imatungo akuogola apika, ndogoilyo imaogola apika namihe akonda.
Hange uyu naukole milunde auekeeye umuundu wakwe mihe, nung'wenso aukete muundu utaki.
Umalaeka numuya wakiza kupuma mitekeelo nila kilunde, nung'wenso aukete umuundu utaki.
Hange akele numalaeka numuya wekiza kupuma pakizindaalo, numalaeka naukete uhumi kumoto. Akamitanga kululi lukulu umalaeka naukete umuundu nuutaki, “ Hola umuundu nuutaki hange wilingele imatambe amizabibu kupuma mumuzabibu nuihe, kunsoko azabibu yitungele yaelya.
Umalaeka wakatwala umuundu wakwe munu mihe hange wikilingeela imaogola azabibu yamihe hange wikaptya mipipa nikulu nilamagae ikuo lang'wi Tunda.
Ipununtelo lamagae aeletulangile kunzi akesale nusakami wikahunuka kupuma mung'wanso mukimo kahatamu afalasi kustadia 1,600.
Hangi nikaona nikiuya ekelengasiilyo kilunde, kikulu nikekete ikuilwa. Aeakole amalaeka mupungate, neakete mapigo mupungate, aemapigo ampelo kunsoko ayayo utaki wang'winda Tunda aiwapika.
Aemine eke naekepumie kumpola yabilauli eye nihalenkanigwe numoto, ekimeka kumpelo nabahali pang'wanso awa naeadoile kukekale nsoko alina lakwe. Aeaambie inubu naeapewe ni Tunda.
Aeakemba wembo wang'wa Musa, mitumi wang'wi Tunda, nuwembo wang'wankolo. Emelemo ako mekolu hange aukoelwa, Mukulu Itunda nuezautemile yehi. mukueli ninzila yakwe yatai, mutemi nuamahe.
Nyenyu nukuleng'wa kuogopa uewe numukulu nukulekulya elina lako? Kunsoko uewe du numutakatifu. Mahe ehi akupembwa nukukulya ntongeela ako kunsoko uewe umuza nintendo yako ilengekile.
Anga kila imakani aya aengozile, hange pang'wanso itakatifu kukila, pang'wanso aeukole usupwo nuawihengi, naiutuguiwe kilunde.
Kupuma pang'wanso pautakatifu kukila akiza amalaeka mupungate naeakete mapigo mupungate, atugae nguo nza, kitani naekimetu numusipi nuazahabu kupilima muikua yao.
Ung'we wao kuawa niapanga anne wikapumilya kuamalaeka mupungate mabakuli mupungate nazahabu naeizue ikuo lang'wi Tunda nuikie ekale na kale.
Pang'wanso itakatifu kukila ulyoki aeluzue kupuma muukulu wang'wi Tunda hange kupuma muuhumi wakwe. Kutile anga nung'we nauhumile kingela sunga mapigo mupungate niamalaeka mupungate naeakaapikeela.
Nikija luli lukulu lukitanga kupuma pangw'anso naeitakatifu hange ikalunga kuamalaeka nemupungate, longola uhunule mihe mabakuli mupungate nikuo lang'wi Tunda.
Umalaeka wang'wandyo aiwendile nukuhunula ibakuli lakwe mihe, enkomele nembee nekete uwai nuutaki akeza kuantu neakete ugomola wakikale, kuawa naeakuiye eadudu akwe.
Umalaeka wakabiile wikahunula ibakuli lakwe mubahali, ikatula anga usakami nuamuntu nukule, hange kila ekeumbe nikipanga nikamubahali kekasha.
Umalaeka wakatatu wekahunula ibakuli lakwe mumongo numunjiilyo ya maze, yekatula sakami. Umalaeka wakatatu wekahunula ibakuli lakwe mumongo numunjiilyo ya maze, yekatula sakami.
Nekija umalaeka nuamaze wekalunga, “Uewe umuhueli - kang'we ukole hange aukole, mtakatifu kunsoko uletile ulamuli uwu.
Kunsoko aeahunue usakami nuahueli nianyakidagu, wikaapa ienso kung'wa usakami, kiko keanonee.”
Nekija ekezindalo kikasusha, “Ee! Umukulu Itunda nutemile muintu yehi, ulamuli wako watai ninkulu.
Umalaeka wakane wakahunula kupuma mibakuli lakwe mulyoa, hange lekapegwa uhumi nuakuasonsa iantu kumoto.
Ekapesigwa nuupyu nuakogopwa, hange ekalumela ulukani lang'wi Tunda, nukete ingulu kumapigo ehi. Ikahila kuungama nukumupa nuanso uukulu.
Umalaeka wakatano wikahunula kupuma mibakuli lakwe mituntu lautemi nilakekale, nekiti kekakunekela utemi wakwe. Aeasiile emino kuwai nuutaki.
Ikamutukila Itunda nuakilunde kunsoko awai wao ninkomele yao, hange akele alongolekile kuhita kuungama kumahiku naeitumile.
Umalaeka nuamutandatu wikahunula kupuma mibakuli lakwe mumongo nuukulu, nuaflati, nimaze akahila kwee kunsoko kunsoko ahume kuzipelya inzila naatemi niapembilye kupuma kilya.
Nikaona nkolo itatu mbee naiyigee anga ntundu niakupuma kunzi umulomo nuizoka ile, ikekale eke, numunyakidagu wauteele.
Inge nkolo yaheng'wi neyeika ilengasiilyo nimakula. Aeenda kuatemi amihe ehi ahume kuilingiila palung'wi kumbita kuluhiku nulukulu lang'wi Tunda nutemile imaintu ehi.
(” Goza! Nzile anga umuhembi! Bahu uyu nukole mumukesha, nuelangaela eang'wenda akwe nsoko waleke kenda kunzi wikipwe nukugoza emenyala akwe.”)
Ikaaleta palung'wi pang'wanso neitangwa ekeebrania amagedoni
Umalaeka nuamupungate wikahunula kupuma mibakuli lakwee umo migulya. Hange luli lukulu lekijeka kupuma patakatifu nukupuma pituntu lautemi iekeze lunga, “Yahila!”
Aeikole nzahi ya welu nulupito, mululumo, nkindo yalupeto, nitetemeko lakutumba - tetemeko ikulu lihe neezekili kupumilamunu mihe kupuma iantu naazie kupuma mihe, ite inge itetemeko ikulu kukila.
Kesale kekolo kekatemanuka mpande itatu, neisale niamahe yekagwa. Hange Itunda wikamukembusha ubabeli numukulu, wikakipa ikesale nikanso ekikombe nekizue imagai kupuma mikuo lakwe nitaki.
Kila ung'wa ihe ikasengeelya imalugulu shanga akigela kwee.
Imbula nkulu amagwe, aekete ulito watalanta, kupuma kilunde ikasima muantu, ekamuzuma Itunda kumapigo ambula amagwe kunsoko ipigo ilo aeibe kukila.
Ung'wiao nuamalaeka mupungate auzile nuukumiila. Nzuu, kulagila ulamuli nuamukosi numukulu nuikie mumaze nedu,
neatemi ihe ituma makani augoolya nung'wenso hangi nimagai naugoolya wakwe neikie mihe agaigwe.
Umalaeka wikanihola kinkolo sunga wikampisha kumbuga hange nekamuona musungu wikie migulya mukikale kikauku naekizue imina aituki. Kikale aikikete matwe mupungate nimbe ikumi.
Umusungu aeukumbilwe ng'wenda wazambalau niyenenkauku imatumbe akwe azahabu magwe ansailo, nelulu mumukono wakwe aeuambie kekombe kazahabu naekizue maintu nakutosha naushapu waugoolya wakwe.
Migula ausu wakwe liandikilwe lina la sili BABELI NUUKULU, IA WAGOOLYA NUYU NUAMAINTU NAUBE WEHI.
Nikaona umusungu uyu augaile sakami auhueli nisakami waawa naeakule kunsoko ang'wa Yesu. Imatungo nae numuine, nekaambwa ukuelwa ukulu.
Kuite umalaeka wika mbela, “Kuneki ukuewe? Kuutambuela endogoelyo amusungu nekikale nikikumuhola, ikekale nekansu nikikete imatwe mupungate nimpembe ikumi.
Ikekale naukiine aekikole, wiketile nitungo nele, kuite ukole ukondile kumankila kupuma mikombo nigila impelo. Hangi ukulongoleka nuushapu. Kuawa naeikie mihe, neminao shangaeandikilwe mumbugulu aupanga kupuma ukuilwa igwe iaunkumbigulu akukoilwa neekakiona ikekalen aeki hoile, kina kikete nitungo, kuite kekole pakupe kiza.
Uwitangwi uwu kunsoko amahala nakete upolo. Imatwe mupungate inge malugulu mupungate papo umusungu aewikae mumo.
Nayo nanso gaa atemi mupungate. Atemi ataano ang'wi, ung'wi ukole, numuya wakile keza, imatungo nuekiza, ukikie matungo maninodaa.
Ikekale naekikole, kuite itungele wikitile, nung'wenso mutemi wamunana, kuite ung'wi wao nuatemi mupungati, hange ulongoe muube.
Impembe niiumi naeuiine inge atemi ikumi neakele kusengelya uutemi, kuite akusengilya uuhumi anga atemi kusaa ing'wiing'wi nekekale.
Awa akete wisiji ung'wi, hangi akumupa ingulu nuuhumi ikekale eki.
Ekituma embita nung'wankolo; kuite ung'wankolo ukuadula kunsoko mukulu waakulu hange mutemi waatemi - hangekukila ng'wenso kukitangwa, ahueli.”
Umalaeka wikambela, “Imazi ayo naeumaine, pang'wanso naewikie umukosi uyo inge intu, utiku mahe nentambu.
Impembe nikumi naeuiine - nukukiila kenso kikale akumubepelwa umukosi uyu. Nienso ekatenda kutula mukia hange wikipwe akumulya umwiile wakwe, hange akulimansilya.
Indogoilyo Itunda uaekile ienso kukenka utimeli wakwe kuigombyi nuakukipa ikikale engulu kumutema sunga inkani yang'wi Tunda nuyukukondaniilya.
Umusungu uyu naumuine inge kesale nekikulu nuutemile muatemi amihe.
Naakeile imaintu aya nikamuona malaika numuya ukusima pihe kupuma kilunde. Nuunso aukete uhumi ukulu, nuhe aiemelikilwe nuukulu wakwe.
Wikalela kululi nulukulu, wikalunga, “Wagwiza, kagwiza, ikesale iko nekikulu Ibabeli! Aina kianza kakikie iahing'wi, hange pang'wanso kila enkolo nimbe ikie, nipang'wanso yaina kila ushapu ninyunyi niyeleta uube.
Kunsoko emahe ehi ang'weza imagai nansula aukosi wakwe nuemuletela ikuo. Eatemi ehi agoolya nung'wenso.
Hange nikija ululi langeza kupuma milunde ikalunga, hegi kug'wanso antu ane, insoko muleke kihangwela mumilandu akwe, ninsoko mulekusingiilya emapigo akwe ehi.
Imelandu akwe ilundie migulya anga kilunde, ni Tunda wakimbuka imelandu akwe nemebe.
Mulepi anga naulepile niang'wi, hange mumulepe kabeele anga naewitumile, mukekombe naukihalekanilye, kuhalinkanya hange kabeele kunsoko akwe.
Anga naiwikuiye nuanso ung'wenso hange aiwikae muusambo, mupi inzago niyendu nuukia kunsoko witunga munkolo akwe. Nikie anga umalaeka hange singamushelwa, hange singakuona uhongelya.
Kuite gwa muluhiku lung'wi imapigo akwe akumulemelya, ninzala. Ukulimansiligwa kumoto, kunsoko amukulu Itunda ukete ingulu, hange mulamuli wakwe.
Eatemi amihe naeagooye nukihangwila palung'wi nuyo akulila nukuhongeelya niikaluona ulyoki lakuzigila kung'wakwe.
Akimeka kule nuyo, kuwoa wauwai wakwe azekengaukia, ukia wakisale nikikulu, Babeli, kesale nekete ingulu! Kusaa eng'wi ulamuli wako wazaa.
Asuluja amihe ehi nukuhongelya kunsoko akwe, kunso kutile nung'wi nukugula insao yakwe hange.
Insao yazahabu, mpia magwe ansailo, lulu, kitani ninza, zambalao, halili, nkauku, aina yehi niyamakota nauwinki nuuza, kila keseme nikampembe andovu, kila kiseme nikeze pigwe kikota niza, shaba, shuma, igwe.
Mdalasini, iungo, uvumba, manemane, ubani, mvinyo, makuta, utu nuuza, ngano, ng'ombe ninkolo, farasi nimagale, niatungwa, ninkolo yaantu.
Inkani nauikete insula kungulu yako ahega kupuma kuwang'wako. Usambo wako wehi nuukengo wahega, shangaukigela kwe.
Iasuluja amaintu aya aealigilye uugole naauloilwe nuanso ukimeka kule kupuma kung'waakwe kunsoko awoa wauwai wakwe, akulela kululi lakuhongeelya.
Akulunga, “Ukia, ukia uo nuukulu nuukumbilwe kitani ninza, zambalao, niye ninkauku, nukulembwa kuzahabu, nukumaintu nansao nilulu.”
Musaa ing'wi ugole wehi nuanso wikahega. Kila nahoza nuameli, kukila bahali, hange ehi niamumaze, hange ehi neituma milimo mubahali.
Aealeile naeaine ulyoki nulakuzigilya kungwakwe, ezelunga, “Kisaleki nikipya nikisale eki nekikulu?”
Ikaguma ulunkunde mumatwe ao, hangi ekalila “ekahung'wa nuliholi nukuhongelya,” Ukia, ukia kisale kikulu kianza kehi, aeakete meli mubahali aeagole nsoko ameli akwe. Kusaa ing'wi ekalimansiligwa.
Lowi migulya akwe, ilunde, unye ahueli itumineanyakidagu, kundogoelyo Itunda waleta ulamuli wanyu migulya akwe.
Umalaeka nuangulu auhumbue igwe anga igwe nikulu nilakusela auligumile mubahali, wikalunga, “kunzila eye, Babeli uyu numukulu, ukugung'wa pihe kulogoha hangi shangaukigela kwee.
Luli lainanda, niakui, iginsi apelembe, nitalumbeta shaa kusiga hangi kitalanyu. Ang'wi umumanyi wehi shangaukigela kitalanyu. Ang'wi ululi lutule shangalukijeka hange kitalanyu.
Uwelu wa ntala shaukumileka mukate akwe. Loli lang'wa Bwana numugoha bibi numusungu niawinga shayukigigwa hangi mukole nako, indogoelyo asuluja ako aeakulu ihe, hange amaha, akongewe kuulogi.
Mukate akwe sakami waanyakidagu niakueli aigee nusakami nuaihe naeabulagilwe migulya nihe.
Pamekakila nanso nikija luli anga mulilo ukulu niiumbe nikulu laantu kilunde ekalunga ilumbi, Uuguni ukulu, ningulu inge yang'wi Tunda witu.
Ulamuli wakwe watai lukulu, kunsoko wamulamula umukosi numukulu numubipiye ihe kugooli wakwe. Witumile kilipo kusakami aitumi akwe, naeumihunue ung'wenso.
Kunkua akabiile, ikalunga “Ilumbi! Ulyoki lepuma kung'wake ikale na kale.”
Ianyampala ao makumi abiile nuunne nimaintu anne nuupanga ikaluma nukukulya Itunda nuikie mituntunlautemi. Aeakulunga, Hueli, Ilumbi!
Papo ululi likapuma mituntu lautemi, ikalunga “Mukulye Itunda witu unye itumi akwe mihe, unye nimuze mekua, ihe niagila umuhimu naaniagila ingulu.”
Papo nikija ululi anga luli liumbe nikulu nilaantu, anga loli lamugugumo nuamaze nedu, hangi anga mugugumo walupito ikalunga, “Ilumbi!” Mkulu Itunda witu, mutemi waawa ehi, nuezutemile.
Nukulumbiye nukuolowa nukumupa ukulu kunsoko awinga nuuli wang'wankolo wazaa, nubibi wawinga ukondile.
Wikagombigwa kutugalwa kitani nikiza nikekumetameta kitani nikiza igebge ntendo niyatai lukulu niyauhueli.
Umalaika wikatambula unene, “Maandike aya: Akembetilwe nianilwe kuwenga wang'wa nkolo.” Kuu uwu wikambila, “Izi nkani yatai nang'wi Tunda.
Aentunile ntongeela amigulu akwe nikakulya. Kuite wikambila, “Uleke kutenda ite! Une numitumi miako nualuna ako nuambile uwihengi nuang'wa Yesu mukulye Itunda, kunsoko uwihengi nuang'wa Yesu nkolo akinyakidagu.”
Hangi nikaona ilunde lakaluguka, hange goza yekatula ukoli farasi nzelu! Nuyu nai umunankie aeukitangwa muhueli hange watai. Lamula itai nukituma embita.
Imiho akwe anga ululeme lamoto, numigulya itwe lakwe ukete ngala yedu. Ukete lina nilaandekilwe migulya akwe nusholimanyile muntu wehi inge ung'wenso duu.
Utugae ng'wenda nunimikilwe musakami nilina lakwe aaukitangwa lukani lang'wi Tunda.
Imajeshi akilunde ae amutyatie migulya afarasi ninzelu, aeatugawe kitani ninza, nzelu hange nza.
Mumulomo wakwe kepuma shege nikitaki nikelima nsilya imahe, nung'wenso wikamusunga kumulanga, kekuo nitaki kung'wi Tunda, wizutemile migulya nihe.
Nung'wenso uandekilwe migulya lang'wenda wakwe numukinama kakwe lina. MUTEMI WA ATEMI HANGI MUKULU WAAKULU.
Aemine malaeka akeze wimekile mulyoa. Auitangile kululi nulukulu inyonyi yehi niyeluma migulya, “Nzii ilingeeli mehi palung'we paludya nulukulu nulang'wi Tunda.
Nzii muliye inyama amutemi, nyama ajemedali, nyama aantu niakulu, nyama afalasi nianankila falasi hange nyama aantu ehi, neidesile niatugwa, niagila umuhimu nawaniagila ingulu.”
Ainekeine ikekale niatemi ihe palungwi nimajeshi ao. Aeipangile kunsoko ambita hange ung'wi naunankie efalasi nijeshi lakwe.
Ikekale kekaambwa numunya kidagu wakwe nuauteele naiwigeeye ilingasilyo muugole wakwe kuilingasilya auakongee awa niasigeeye ugomola wakikali nawa naiakuiye ududu wakwe. Ehi muubiile akagung'wa akizeapanga milule la moto nuakiigwe nikibiliti.
Awa naeasigile akabulagwa neshege naikipumile kumulomo wang'wa ung'wi wao naunankie migulya la falasi. Inyunyi yehi aiilie imeimba namiile ao.
Hange nikaona makika akusima kupuma milunde akeze akete nifunguo yikombo nigila anga mpelo numunyololo ukulu kumuko wakwe.
Aeuliambile izoka ilo, nzoka nikale, ibilisi ang'wi Shetani, nukumukulya myaka elfu.
Aemugumile mikombo nigila anga mpelo, akalitunga nukuliikila ugomola migulya lakwe. Iye aeituile insoko kina alekekumakongela imahe hange kupikela myaka elfu nuekikie. Anga yakila pangwanso, ukolekelwa widesi kumatungo mashenyi.
Hange aimine matuntu autemi. Naeamikae ingi wawa naeapewe uhumi nuakulamula. Uu lukulu amine ifalasi niawa naeatemilwe imatwe kunsoko awihengi wang'wa Yesu nukulukani lang'wi Tunda. Nesinga aiakikuiye ekekale ang'wi udubu wakwe, hange aeahitile kusengeelya ugomola nuusu wao ang'wi mumukono. Ikapembya muupanga, hangi ikapembya palung'wi nuuKilisto kumyaka elfu.
Eashi nueasigile shaakiza kuupanga sunga myaka elfu ikahila. Uyu inge uiuki wang'wandyo.
Mupegwe nuutakatifu inge muntu wehi nukumuhola enafsi muantu anga awa. Yukulula niakuhani ang'wi Tunda nuKilisto nukutemya nuyo myaka elfu.
imatungo myaka elfu niikatimela, umulugu wekaluguelwa kupuma mukitungo kakwe.
Ukupuma nukuakongola. Iamataifa munindo inne niyamihe - Gogu nemagogu - kualeta palungwe kunsoko ambita. Akulula idu anga umuhanganga wamubahali.
Aeindile migulya mutambalale nihe ikamipilimilya enkambe naahueli kosale kaulowa. Kuite umotowekiza kupuma kilunde nukulagiilya.
Mulugu ushetani nae u kongee, augumilwe mkati a moto nilakeigwe nikibiliti, mungwanso kikali numunyakidagu nuwautele aeagumilwe. Akagigwa mung'wi nuutiku ikale nakale.
Hange nikaona ituntu lautemi kikulu kelu nuyu naewikie mung'wanso. Ihe ni lunde yekamanka kuli kuhega kuukulu wakwe, kuite aeagila angalyoma nianso kulongola.
Aenuaine niakule - angulu nawa nisingo amuhimu imekile pituntu lautemi, nimbigulu yikalungulwa. Hange ekalugulwa - imbugulu aupanga. iashi ekalamula kukela eki naekandekilwe mumbugulu, ikinyamulimo kao iki naeitumile.
Ebahali ekaapumya eashi naeakole mukate akwe. Nshanialungu aeapumilye iashi naeakole mukati akwe hange iashi ikalamulwa anga uu naiitenda.
Insha nuulungu yekagung'wa mukate niule la moto. Iyi insha akabiili - ilule la moto.
Ang'wi ilina lawihi shangaligee mumbugulu aupanga, augumilwe milule la moto.
Hange nikaona ilunde ipya nihe mpya, kunsoko ilunde lang'wandyo nihe nang'wandyo yakeile, nibahali ekutile hange.
Nikakiona kisale kitakatifu Yerusalemu nempya, naeisimile pihe kupuma kilunde kung'wi Tunda, nuuziipigwe anga ubibi alusi nunoneigwe kunsoko amugoha.
Aenigule luli lukulu kupuma mituntu lautemi ikalunga Goza! Ulikalo lang'wi Tunda lukole niantu, nung'wenso ukikie palung'we nusese. Akutula antu akwe, nung'wenso Itunda akutula nienso hange ukutula Itunda wao.
Ukuapyagula uliholi lehi kupuma mumiho ao, ikakutile angansha hange, ang'wi kuhongelya, ang'wi kukila, ang'wi uwai, imakani akale akeile.
Nuanso naewikie migulya mituntu lautemi wikalunga, “Goza! Kumatenda imakani mehi kutula mapya.” Aulieye, Andeke ile kunsoko inkani izi yakulukulu nitai.”
Aumbie, “Imakani ayaite aiakeile! Une ni Alfa hange ne Omega nitangi hange nikwangu. Kuwihe nukuhung'wa inyota kumupa wang'we bila uguli kupuma munjiilyo yamaze naupanga.
Nuanso nuekadula ukumasala aya ehi, hange kutula ni Tunda wakwe, nung'wenso ukutula ng'waane.
Kuite anga uu niyele kuawa niao, nisha ahuie abepilani, abulagi, agoolyi, alogi, akulya adudu, hange niateele ehi, ikianza kao kikutula milule la moto nuakibiliti nuesonsa. Nanso yeyo nsha akabiile.
Ung'we nuamalaeka mupungate wikeza kung'wane ung'wi naukete mabakuli mupungate naiizue mapigo mupungate nampelo nukulunga, “Nzuu apa. Kulagila ubibi alusi, musungu nung”wankolo.
Hange wikanihola kule ikinkolo kulugulu lukulu hange lulipu hange wikandagiila kisale nikitakatifu, Yerusalemu, ukusima pihe kupuma kilunde kung'wi Tunda.
Yerusalemu aeukete nuukulu nuang'wi Tunda, hange uzaa wakwe aeanga kito niansailo, anga igwe nilakeoo nikiza nikayapisi.
Aeukete ikiligo ikulu, ulepu aukete milango kumi na mbiili palung'wi niamalaeka kumi na mbeele mumilango itaatu, inkika nakutakama milango itatu, ninkika nakung'weli milango itaatu.
Inkika nakilya milango itatu, inkika nahukuma milango itaatu, ninkika nakutakama milango itaatu, ninkika nakung'weli milango itaatu.
Imakiligo nakisale aeakite emisingi ikumi na mbiili numigulya lakwe aeakole mina kumi na mbiile naalungwa kumi na mbiili nang'wankolo.
Ung'wi ao nauligitilye nune aukete ugemeeli wamilanga aeizipigwe kuzahabu kunsoko akugemeelya kisale, imelango akwe nimakiligo akwe.
Ikesale aekeikilwe mukate amilaba; ulepu wakwe aewipyani nuugale wakwe. Augemeeye ikesale kuigemelyi nuamilanga, stadia 12,000 kuulepu ulepu wakwe, ugale, nekimo aiyimpyani.
Uu uuu augemeeye nikiligo lakwe, ukomu wakwe ae dhiraa 144 kuugeeli nuakiuntu (nuo nuanso gaa ugemeeli nuamalaeka).
Ikiligo aelezengilwe kuyapisi nikisale nekekete zahabu nenza, anga ekioo nekiza.
Imesingi nikiligo aepambilwe kela eaina nigwe lansailo. Nelang'wandyo aeyapisi nelakabiili aeyakuti samawi, nilakataatu ae kalkedon, nilakanne zumaridi.
Nilaakataano sardoniki, nilamutandatu akili, nilamupungate krisolintho, nilamunana zabarajadi nilakenda yakuti namanjano nilikumi krisoproso, nilikumineng'wi hiakintho, nela kumi nambiili amethisto.
Imelango kumi na mbiili ailulu kuminambiili, kila umulango aeuzepigwe kupuma mululu ing'wi. Isale niinino niakisole aezahabu ninza, nigee anga kioo nikiza.
Singa aemine itekeelo lehi mukati nakisale, kunsoko Itunda numukulu, nutemil iintu yehi nung'wankolo inge itekeelo lakwe.
Ikesale shangaaekeloilwe anga lyoa ang'wi ng'weli kunsoko akumileka migulya lakwe kunsoko ukulu wang'wi Tunda aeumelikile migulya lakwe nito lakwe ng'waankolo.
Imahe akugenda kuwelu wakisale kiko. Iatemi amunkumbulu akuleta ukuulu wao mukati akwe.
Imilango akwe singa ikilugailwa, imelango namung'wi ikatile anga utiku pang'wanso.
Akuleta ukulu nilikulyo lamahe mukati akwe,
hange kutile nikishapu nikekingila mukate akwe ang'wi wehi nuanso nukituma ikani lamenyala ang'wi uteele singa ukingila, inge wawadu neminaa andekilwe mumbugulu aupanga nikang'wankolo.
Hange umalaeka wikandageela mongo nuamazi naupanga, mazi naeakumelegenta anga nuabilauri. Ae akuhuma kupuma pituntu lautemi nilang'wi Tunda nile nilang'wankolo.
Kukeela pakatekate akisale nikenino, pakesale. Kukela ninde amongo aelikole ikota laupanga, nuukutuga aina kumi nambiile niyankali, hange letuga kila ung'weli. Imatutu ni kota kunsoko akumigwa eanyakelungu.
Hange ikakutile anga kezume kwee. Ituntu lautemi nilang'wi Tunda nelenilang'wankolo. Ikalekole mukate akisale, neitumi akwe akumitumila.
Akumuona uaso wakwe nelina lakwe lekutula migulya ausu wao.
Ikakutie anga utiku kwee, hange ikakutile anga uula nuawelu nuantala ang'wi lyoa kunsoko Itunda mukulu ukuamilekela migulya lao. Neenso ikidesa ikale na kale.
Umalaeka wikambela, “Inkani izi yakuhuelwa hange tai. Itunda numukulu nuankolo yanyakidagu aeumutumile umalaika wakwe kualagiila itumi akwe nekekapumila ite pakupe.
Goza! nekakaya keza! Ukembetilwe uyu nuekaikulya inkani yakidagu nikambugulu eye!”
Une, Yohana, nene ainigule nukuona emakani aya. Naenigule nukuona, aengwie pihe unene ntongeela amigulu ang'wamalaeka kumukulya, umalaeka naundagie imakani aya.
Wikambila, “Uleke kutenda ite! Une numitumi miako, palung'wi nealuna ako anyakedagu, palung'wi nawaniekulya inkani yambugulu eye. Mukulye Itunda!”
Wikambila, “Ulekekuekila ugomola inkani yakidagu nikambugulu eye, endogoelyo imatungo apika.
Numugila etai ukulongoleka kutula mugila angatai. Numushapu mumanyisigwa, nualongoleke kutula mushapu keumanyisigwa. Nukete etai, nualongoleke kutula ukete itai. Numutakatifu, nualongoleka kutula mtakatifu.
Goza! Kukaya kiza. Ikinyamulimo kane kikole palung'wi nunyenye, kumupa kila ung'wi ao anga keko naiwirumile.
Une ni Alfa hange ni Omega, Tangi hange Kwangu, ng'wandyo nimpelo.
Akembetilwe awaite ni ojaa iang'wenda ao insoko kina apegwe ekulu nakulya kupuma pikota laupanga nukingila mukisale kukiila pamulango.
Kunzi ikole mbwa, alogi, agoolya, abulagi, akulya adudu nuyu nuloilwe kihenga uwihengi nuauteele
Une, neYesu, namutuma umalaeka wane kuatambuela imakani aya mumatekeelo. Une nimulinuautugwa wang'wa Daudi. Nzota nakidaudau nemelegenta.
Nkolo nubibi nuwinga watunga. Nzuu! Nuyu migule walunga, “Nzuu! Wihi nukete inyota, nuaze, hange wihi nukete enzula, naapate imazi aupanga nikanda.
Kumuila kila umuntu nukija inkani niakidagu niyambugulu eye. Ang'wi wihe nukungeelya imapigo naandikilwe mumbugulu eye.
Ang'wi muntu wihi nukuiheja inkani mumbugulu eyenakidagu, Itunda ukuheja ikeanza kakwe mikota laupanga hange mukisale nikitakatifu, impola yakwe niiandekilwe mukati ambugulu eye.
Nuanso nuihengile inkani izi ukulunga, “Ee! Kukaya kiza.” Huela! Nzuu, uYesu mukulu.
Ukende ukulu nuang'wa Yesu utule kukila muntu. Huela.
